# Kerf тАФ Roadmap

**Status glyphs:** `тЬЕ shipped` ┬╖ `ЁЯЪз in flight` ┬╖ `ЁЯФ┤ not started`

---

## North Star

**The most comprehensive CAD on Earth тАФ a single tool in which a person can design *anything*.** Mechanical engineering, electronics, PCB, architecture, civil engineering, drafting, jewelry, automotive тАФ and every other CAD sector, including the small and niche ones. We are doing **everything**. Nothing here is "cut." Lower priority means *later*, not *dropped*.

This is a **priority-ordered** roadmap, not a date-ordered or effort-ordered one. The tiers (P0 тЖТ P3) express sequence and leverage: which items earn the most credibility per unit of work.

Kerf is dual-licensed: the OSS core (MIT) and the hosted-tier code under `packages/kerf-{billing,cloud}/` + `src/cloud/`.

### Why chat-driven CAD works

Kerf is **chat-driven** CAD. Every capability is designed around one constraint:

> *Can the LLM produce and re-edit this deliverable through a text-native tool, and verify the result?*

Professional CAD is overcomplicated mostly because of command-discovery affordances (ribbons, palettes, wizards) that an LLM does not need. Kerf ships professional **capability** while deliberately not shipping professional **UI complexity**. This makes the roadmap shorter than it looks: many "pro features" are UX wrappers around a parametric core we expose as a text schema + LLM tool + verifier.

**Hard guardrail:** simplification is about *authoring mechanics only*. It is never an excuse to drop a domain or to skimp on correctness, output formats, or standards compliance. Those are *more* important under an LLM, not less.

---

## Platform foundation

The sector work only matters if you **own your work, are not locked in, and can run Kerf wherever you want**. Four commitments, all decided:

1. **Every cloud project is a real git repository** тАФ `git clone`-able with stock git, no special client. Large or binary files are auto-detected and stored with a small in-git pointer. Version control is two complementary layers: fine-grained automatic file history *and* deliberate, shareable commits with GitHub sync.

2. **One client, cloud by default, easy optional self-host** тАФ `pip install kerf` for the hosted cloud; `pip install 'kerf[server]'` + bring-your-own-Postgres + `kerf serve` for self-host. Same client, same data model, both paths first-class.

3. **Portability is the anti-lock-in guarantee** тАФ `kerf sync` mirrors to a local folder with two-way sync; `kerf export` / `kerf import` produce and ingest a plain file tree. Moving a project between cloud and self-host is painless.

4. **A fully-local / offline desktop app is committed but demand-gated** тАФ portability + two-way sync + easy self-host is the complete launch answer to "I want to own my data." The standalone offline desktop build is sequenced behind real demand.

---

## What shipped

### Latest delta тАФ 2026-05-31

**ELEC-OPTOCOUPLER-CTR** тЬЕ тАФ Optocoupler isolation circuit analysis: given LED forward current IF, CTR(min/typ/max), output pull-up R_L, supply Vcc, and load capacitance C_L, computes IC (min/typ/max), saturation threshold IC_sat = Vcc/R_L, saturation verdict, Vout_low = Vce_sat, Vout_high = Vcc, output rise/fall time, and headroom factor. `analyze_optocoupler(OptocouplerSpec, CircuitSpec) -> OptocouplerReport` in `kerf_electronics.optocoupler_ctr`. Dataclasses: `OptocouplerSpec` (model, IF_mA, CTR_min_percent, CTR_typ_percent, CTR_max_percent, Vce_sat_V, IF_max_mA, Vf_typ_V=1.2, t_rise_us_at_Rl=(2.0, 1000)); `CircuitSpec` (Vcc_out_V, R_pullup_ohm, C_load_pF=20.0, R_LED_series_ohm, V_LED_drive_V); `OptocouplerReport` (IC_min_mA, IC_typ_mA, IC_max_mA, IC_saturation_mA, saturated_min_case, Vout_low_V, Vout_high_V, t_rise_us, t_fall_us, headroom_factor_min, warnings, honest_caveat). Algorithm: IC = CTR/100 ├Ч IF_mA (IEC 60747-5-5 ┬з6.3); IC_sat = Vcc/R_L ├Ч 1000 [mA]; saturated_min_case = (IC_min >= IC_sat); headroom = IC_min/IC_sat; t_rise = max(2.2├ЧR_L├ЧC_L, t_rise_spec├ЧR_L_actual/R_L_spec) [┬╡s]; t_fall = t_rise (symmetric R-C model). Warns: IF > IF_max (over-drive); NOT saturated (IC_min < IC_sat, suggests fix); headroom < 2.0 (aging margin); IF mismatch (circuit-derived IF vs spec IF > 25%). `elec_analyze_optocoupler` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 68 tests green. HONEST: LINEAR CTR MODEL ONLY тАФ IC = CTR/100 ├Ч IF; real CTR vs IF is non-linear (peaks at moderate IF, falls at extremes); TEMPERATURE AND LIFETIME DERATING NOT MODELLED тАФ CTR degrades 30тАУ50% over LED lifetime at elevated temperature (Avago AN-5078 ┬з4.3); always derate CTR to the datasheet minimum at maximum rated temperature (NOT the 25┬░C value); Vce_sat is a fixed datasheet spec (actual depends on IC + temperature); rise/fall time is an RC estimate (2.2├ЧR_L├ЧC_L) тАФ minority-carrier storage NOT modelled; for high-speed designs use t_PLH/t_PHL from the datasheet at exact R_L and V_CC; isolation voltage (V_IORM, IEC 60747-5-5 creepage/clearance) NOT checked. Refs: Vishay Application Note AN-38 "Optocoupler Output Response Time"; Avago/Broadcom Application Note 5078 "Using Optocouplers"; IEC 60747-5-5:2007 ┬з6.3 тАФ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/optocoupler_ctr.py`.

**ELEC-ZENER-TC-DRIFT** тЬЕ тАФ Zener voltage drift over temperature using temperature coefficient TC (mV/┬░C). Models the Vz vs T curve which has a zero-TC crossing near 5.6 V (above: positive TC dominated by avalanche; below: negative TC dominated by Zener tunneling). `compute_zener_drift(ZenerSpec, OperatingSpec) -> ZenerDriftReport` in `kerf_electronics.zener_tc_drift`. Dataclasses: `ZenerSpec` (Vz_nominal_V, TC_mV_per_C, test_current_mA, test_temp_C=25.0); `OperatingSpec` (current_mA, ambient_temp_C_min, ambient_temp_C_max); `ZenerDriftReport` (Vz_at_min_temp_V, Vz_at_max_temp_V, Vz_drift_total_V, Vz_drift_percent, current_dependence_warning, recommendation, honest_caveat). Algorithm: rZтЙИ0.01├ЧVz/Iz_test [╬й] (Vishay AN-2014-3 ┬з2.2); ╬ФVz_current=rZ├Ч(Iz_opтИТIz_test) [V]; Vz(T)=(Vz_nom+╬ФVz_current)+TC├Ч10тБ╗┬│├Ч(TтИТT_test) [V]; drift_percent=100├Ч|Vz(T_max)тИТVz(T_min)|/Vz_nom; current deviation >50% triggers warning. Recommendation: drift>5% тЖТ suggest 5.6V near-zero-TC Zener (BZX55C5V6, 1N5232B) or bandgap Vref IC (LM4040, ADR4550, LT6656). Physical basis: Zener tunneling (Vz<5V, negative TC, band-gap narrowing тИВEg/тИВT<0 per Varshni equation); avalanche impact ionisation (Vz>7V, positive TC, phonon scattering reduces carrier mean free path); mixed regime 5тАУ7V with TCтЙИ0 near 5.6V (device-process-specific). `elec_compute_zener_drift` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: LINEAR TC MODEL ONLY тАФ real Vz vs T is mildly quadratic in the 5тАУ7V transition region (second-order deviation ┬▒0.1тАУ0.3 mV / 100┬░C, Sze ┬з4.5 Fig. 4.5-6); TC is current-dependent (┬▒10тАУ20% at significantly different Iz); part-to-part TC spread ┬▒30тАУ50% for C-suffix Zeners; thermal self-heating NOT modelled (T_j=T_amb+╬╕JA├ЧP_Z, ╬╕JA~300тАУ600┬░C/W for DO-35/SOD-80); rZ linearisation valid only within ~50% of Iz_test; zero-TC crossing is device/manufacturer-specific. Refs: S. M. Sze "Physics of Semiconductor Devices" 3e ┬з4.5; H&H ┬з2.2.4 Table 2.1; Vishay AN-2014-3 ┬з2.4; ON AN-961 ┬з3 тАФ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/zener_tc_drift.py`.

**ELEC-ZENER-CLAMP** тЬЕ тАФ Zener-diode voltage clamp + series resistor design for DC supply rail regulation. `design_zener_clamp(ZenerClampSpec) -> ZenerClampReport` in `kerf_electronics.zener_clamp_design`. Dataclasses: `ZenerClampSpec` (V_in_min_V, V_in_max_V, V_zener_V, I_load_min_A, I_load_max_A, V_zener_tolerance_pct=5.0, I_zener_knee_A=0.001); `ZenerClampReport` (R_series_ohm, R_series_power_W, I_zener_max_A, P_zener_max_W, recommended_zener_package, recommended_R_E12_ohm, regulation_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: R = (V_in_max тИТ V_Z) / (I_load_min + I_knee); V_Z_max = V_Z├Ч(1+tol/100); I_Z_max = (V_in_max тИТ V_Z_max)/R тИТ I_load_min; P_Z_design = V_Z ├Ч I_Z_max ├Ч 1.25 (25% derating margin per Vishay AN-2014-3 ┬з3); P_R = (V_in_max тИТ V_Z) ├Ч (I_Z_max + I_load_min). Zener package thresholds: 0.4 W (DO-35/SOD-80, BZX55 series), 0.5 W (DO-41, BZX79), 1 W (DO-41/BZX85, 1N4728тАУ1N4764), 3 W (DO-201/P600), 5 W (SOT-89/TO-252). E12 series resistor from IEC 60063 (round up for conservative power). `electronics_design_zener_clamp` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 60 tests green. HONEST: SIMPLE LINEAR SHUNT REGULATOR ONLY тАФ wasted power = (V_in_maxтИТV_Z)├ЧI_R_total regardless of load draw; at zero load ALL current flows through Zener; for I_load > 100 mA or efficiency-sensitive rails STRONGLY prefer LDO linear regulator (LM1117, MCP1700) or switching buck converter; Zener incremental resistance rZ NOT modelled (╬ФV_out = rZ├Ч╬ФI_Z тАФ typical rZ 7тАУ20 ╬й for 5 V / 400 mW parts тАФ use TL431 or shunt reference IC for tight regulation); temperature coefficient of V_Z NOT modelled (below ~5 V TC is negative, above ~5.6 V positive; тЙИ5.1 V Zeners have ~0 TC); 25% margin is steady-state тАФ pulse/transient peaks require JEDEC JESD51-2 transient thermal impedance analysis; static regulation = 2├Чtol% only (dynamic line/load from rZ excluded). Refs: Horowitz & Hill "Art of Electronics" 3e ┬з2.2.4; Vishay Application Note AN-2014-3 тАФ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/zener_clamp_design.py`.

**ELEC-OP-AMP-OFFSET-DRIFT** тЬЕ тАФ Op-amp input offset voltage and temperature drift calculator for precision instrumentation design. `compute_op_amp_drift(OpAmpSpec, CircuitSpec, error_budget_pct=0.1) -> OpAmpOffsetReport` in `kerf_electronics.op_amp_offset_drift`. Dataclasses: `OpAmpSpec` (Vos_typ_uV, Vos_drift_uV_per_C, T_ambient_min_C, T_ambient_max_C, T_reference_C=25.0); `CircuitSpec` (gain_VV, signal_full_scale_V); `OpAmpOffsetReport` (Vos_at_T_min_uV, Vos_at_T_max_uV, Vos_max_input_referred_uV, Vos_max_output_referred_mV, error_pct_of_FS, within_spec, recommended_op_amp_class, honest_caveat). Algorithm: Vos(T) = Vos_typ + TC_Vos ├Ч (T тИТ T_ref) (TI SLOA069 ┬з3 Eq. 3-1); worst-case evaluates all 4 (┬▒drift ├Ч ┬▒endpoint) combinations and takes max absolute; Vos_max_IR = max(|Vos(T_min)|, |Vos(T_max)|); Vos_OR_mV = gain ├Ч Vos_max_IR / 1000; error_pct = 100 ├Ч (Vos_OR_mV/1000) / FS. Class thresholds: "chopper" (TC_Vos тЙд 0.05 ┬╡V/┬░C, e.g. AD8551, MAX420); "zero-drift" (тЙд 0.1 ┬╡V/┬░C, e.g. OPA188, LTC2050); "precision" (тЙд 1.0 ┬╡V/┬░C, e.g. OPA227, LT1012); "standard" (> 1.0 ┬╡V/┬░C). Recommendation: "chopper" when error тЙе 10├Ч budget; "precision" when over budget; confirm class from TC when in budget. Reference design (task spec): Vos=100 ┬╡V, drift=2 ┬╡V/┬░C, T=[0..70]┬░C, gain=100, FS=5V тЖТ Vos(T_max)=190 ┬╡V, output=19 mV, error=0.38%. `electronics_compute_op_amp_drift` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: linear drift model ONLY тАФ Vos(T)=Vos_typ+TC_Vos├Ч╬ФT; real drift is non-linear and asymmetric (TI SLOA069 Fig 3-2); Vos_typ is nominal (not guaranteed тАФ use Vos_max for design margin); **1/f (flicker) noise contribution to DC offset NOT modelled** (can dominate sub-Hz BJT-input amps); **PSRR/CMRR cross-talk effects OUT OF SCOPE** (╬ФVos_PSRR = ╬ФVPS/PSRR must be added separately); resistor TC mismatch in feedback network adds gain-drift error not captured. Refs: TI "Op Amp Errors" SLOA069 ┬з3 Eq. 3-1; Analog Devices AN-580 ┬з1; OPA188 / AD8551 / LT1012 datasheets тАФ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/op_amp_offset_drift.py`.

**ELEC-INDUCTOR-CORE-SAT** тЬЕ тАФ Inductor core saturation checker. `check_inductor_saturation(InductorCoreSpec, InductorCurrentSpec) -> CoreSaturationReport` in `kerf_electronics.inductor_core_saturation`. Dataclasses: `InductorCoreSpec` (material: "ferrite_3C95"|"ferrite_3F36"|"powdered_iron_-26"|"sendust"|"NiFe50", A_e_mm2, l_e_mm, B_sat_mT, mu_r); `InductorCurrentSpec` (turns_N, I_dc_A, I_ripple_peak_to_peak_A, temperature_C=25.0); `CoreSaturationReport` (B_peak_mT, B_sat_mT, saturation_margin_pct, saturated, recommended_max_I_dc_A, honest_caveat). Algorithm: I_pk = I_dc + I_ripple_pp/2; B_pk = ╬╝тВА┬╖╬╝_r┬╖N┬╖I_pk/l_e (Ampere's law, uniform closed path); saturation_margin = (B_sat тИТ B_pk)/B_sat ├Ч 100; saturated = B_pk >= B_sat; recommended_max_I_dc = max(0, 0.99┬╖B_sat┬╖l_e/(╬╝тВА┬╖╬╝_r┬╖N) тИТ I_ripple/2). Temperature derating for ferrite materials: piecewise-linear (100┬░CтЖТтИТ15%, 125┬░CтЖТтИТ25%, 150┬░CтЖТтИТ40%, 200┬░CтЖТтИТ50%) per Ferroxcube 3C95/3F36 datasheets; not applied to powder-iron/Sendust/NiFe. `electronics_check_inductor_saturation` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 26 tests green. HONEST: fringing flux ignored (gapped cores need Dowell/Erickson ┬з15.3 gap fringing correction); ╬╝_r assumed constant (real ferrite ╬╝_r rolls off substantially in the knee region BEFORE B_sat тАФ model over-estimates B_pk conservatively; use nonlinear B-H curve for precision); non-ferrite B_sat derating NOT modelled; winding I┬▓R temperature rise NOT accounted; AC core losses (Steinmetz) NOT computed тАФ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/inductor_core_saturation.py`. Refs: Erickson "Power Electronics" 3e ┬з15; McLyman "Transformer and Inductor Design Handbook" 4e ┬з10; Ferroxcube 3C95/3F36 datasheets; Magnetics Inc. Powder Core Catalog ┬з3.

**ELEC-FET-SOA-CHECK** тЬЕ тАФ MOSFET Safe Operating Area (SOA) checker. `check_fet_soa(FETSpec, FETOperatingPoint) -> FETSOAReport` in `kerf_electronics.fet_soa_check`. Dataclasses: `FETSpec` (part_number, V_DSS_max_V, I_D_continuous_A, I_D_pulsed_A, R_DS_on_mOhm, T_J_max_C, R_theta_JA_K_per_W, P_D_max_W); `FETOperatingPoint` (V_DS_V, I_D_A, pulse_duration_ms, duty_cycle, T_ambient_C); `FETSOAReport` (within_soa, P_diss_W, T_junction_estimate_C, soa_violation_modes, headroom_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: P_diss = V_DS ├Ч I_D ├Ч duty; T_J = T_amb + P_diss ├Ч R_╬╕JA (Jedec JESD51 single-node); violation checks: V_DSS_exceeded (V_DS > V_DSS_max), I_D_continuous_exceeded (duty==1.0 AND I_D > I_D_continuous), I_D_pulsed_exceeded (duty<1.0 AND I_D > I_D_pulsed), T_J_exceeded (T_J > T_J_max), P_D_exceeded (P_diss > P_D_max); headroom_pct = (1 тИТ max(utilisation_ratios)) ├Ч 100. `electronics_check_fet_soa` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 30 tests green. HONEST: LINEARISED SOA only тАФ real datasheet SOA curves (IRF Hexfet Designer's Manual ┬з5 Fig 5-1) are non-linear in the thermal-limited and second-breakdown regions; pulse-width SOA NOT interpolated (short pulses allow higher peak I_D├ЧV_DS before the thermal integral exceeds the die's transient thermal capacity); second-breakdown (avalanche/UIS) NOT explicitly modelled as a separate boundary тАФ for inductive turn-off verify E_AS = ┬╜┬╖L┬╖I_peak┬▓ < rated E_AS; thermal model is single-node JESD51 steady-state R_╬╕JA (not transient Z_╬╕JC(t)); R_DS_on is room-temperature datasheet value (actual R_DS_on increases with T_J per Infineon AN 2015-11); switching losses (turn-on, turn-off, gate charge) NOT included in P_diss тАФ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/fet_soa_check.py`. Refs: IRF Hexfet Designer's Manual ┬з5; IPC-9701A; Jedec JESD51-1; Infineon AN 2015-11.

**ELEC-LDO-DROPOUT-CHECK** тЬЕ тАФ LDO linear regulator dropout and thermal compliance checker. `check_ldo_dropout(LDOSpec) -> LDODropoutReport` in `kerf_electronics.ldo_dropout_check`. Dataclasses: `LDOSpec` (V_out_V, V_in_min_V, V_in_max_V, I_load_A, dropout_voltage_at_max_load_mV, junction_to_ambient_thermal_resistance_K_per_W, T_ambient_C=25, T_max_junction_C=125); `LDODropoutReport` (headroom_min_mV, dropout_compliant, power_dissipation_W, junction_temp_estimate_C, thermal_compliant, efficiency_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: headroom_mV = (V_in_min тИТ V_out) ├Ч 1000; dropout_compliant = headroom_mV > dropout_spec_mV (strict); P_diss = (V_in_max тИТ V_out) ├Ч I_load; T_j = T_ambient + P_diss ├Ч R_╬╕ja (Jedec JESD51 single-node); thermal_compliant = T_j < T_max_junction; efficiency = 100 ├Ч V_out / V_in_max (pessimistic). `electronics_check_ldo_dropout` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 54 tests green. HONEST: quiescent current I_Q NOT included (dominates at light load тАФ TI Power Ref ┬з3.2.3); transient headroom NOT checked (PSRR roll-off + input cap droop during load steps; add тЙе100тАУ200 mV guard-band per Sandler ┬з4.4); output capacitor stability NOT verified (ESR window requirement); thermal model is ╬╕ja worst-case (╬╕jb+╬╕jc paths not modelled); efficiency = V_out/V_in_max ignores I_Q тАФ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/ldo_dropout_check.py`. Refs: TI Power Reference Manual ┬з3; Sandler "Switch-Mode Power Supplies" ┬з4; Jedec JESD51-1.

**ELEC-DC-DC-CONVERTER-RIPPLE** тЬЕ тАФ Output voltage ripple ╬ФV_out (peak-to-peak) for a buck DC-DC converter in Continuous Conduction Mode (CCM). `compute_buck_ripple(BuckConverterSpec) -> ConverterRippleReport` in `kerf_electronics.dc_dc_ripple`. Dataclasses: `BuckConverterSpec` (V_in_V, V_out_V, I_load_A, switching_freq_Hz, L_uH, C_out_uF, C_ESR_mOhm); `ConverterRippleReport` (delta_iL_pp_A, delta_V_out_pp_mV, delta_V_capacitor_mV, delta_V_ESR_mV, duty_cycle, output_ripple_pct, honest_caveat). Algorithm: D = V_out/V_in; ╬ФiL = (V_inтИТV_out)┬╖D/(L┬╖f_sw); ╬ФV_cap = ╬ФiL/(8┬╖C┬╖f_sw); ╬ФV_ESR = ╬ФiL┬╖ESR; ╬ФV_out = ╬ФV_cap + ╬ФV_ESR (worst-case linear sum per Erickson ┬з2.4). CCM validity: iL_min = I_load тИТ ╬ФiL/2 > 0 flagged; small-ripple approximation warning when ╬ФiL/(2┬╖I_load) > 30%; ESR-dominance flag when ESR > 1/(4╧А┬╖C┬╖f_sw). `electronics_compute_buck_ripple` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_electronics/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: CCM only тАФ DCM (iL_min < 0) NOT modelled; small-ripple approximation (Erickson ┬з2.1) breaks above 30% load variation; D = V_out/V_in is ideal (no deadtime, body-diode drop, or min-on-pulse); ESR assumed resistive/frequency-flat (use datasheet ESR at f_sw); ╬ФV_out is pessimistic linear sum (RSS is ~3тАУ15% less pessimistic) тАФ `packages/kerf-electronics/src/kerf_electronics/dc_dc_ripple.py`. Refs: Erickson "Fundamentals of Power Electronics" 3e ┬з2.1, ┬з2.4 Eq 2.34+2.36; Sandler "Power Electronics" ┬з3; TI SLVA477.

**MOLD-RUNNER-DIAMETER-OPTIMIZE** тЬЕ тАФ Optimal cold-runner diameter recommendation using the Beaumont (2007) ┬з6.5 empirical formula D=(W^0.25├ЧтИЪL)/3.7, balancing fill pressure against cold-runner waste. `optimize_runner_diameter(RunnerOptimizeSpec) -> RunnerOptimizeReport` in `kerf_mold.runner_diameter_optimize`. Dataclasses: `RunnerOptimizeSpec` (part_weight_g, runner_length_mm, polymer_grade, gate_count=1); `RunnerOptimizeReport` (recommended_diameter_mm, beaumont_diameter_mm, cold_runner_waste_g, fill_pressure_estimate_MPa, polymer_specific_adjustment, honest_caveat). Algorithm: D_base=(W_eff^0.25├ЧтИЪL)/3.7 where W_eff=W/gate_count; material-viscosity adjustment: ABS+10%, PC+15% (highly viscous), PP-5% (low viscosity), PA66┬▒0%; D clamped to [1.5, 16.0] mm. Cold-runner waste = ╧А┬╖(D/2)┬▓┬╖L ├Ч ╧Б_polymer/1000 [g]; polymer densities: ABS 1.05, PC 1.20, PP 0.91, PA66 1.14 g/cm┬│ (Menges 2001 Table 2.1). Fill-pressure proxy: PтЙИK_mat┬╖L/D^4 (Hagen-Poiseuille analogy, order-of-magnitude only). `mold_optimize_runner_diameter` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 28 tests green. HONEST: empirical formula only тАФ NOT a full Hele-Shaw or Cross-WLF rheological simulation; optimises a SINGLE runner segment for one gate тАФ does NOT optimise filling balance in multi-cavity molds (use mold_check_runner_balance + mold_generate_runner_layout for multi-cavity networks); fill-pressure estimate is order-of-magnitude proxy only; cold-runner waste assumes cylindrical cross-section (trapezoidal/half-round runners have different volumes); confirm with Moldflow/Moldex3D/SigmaSoft fill simulation and mold trial тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/runner_diameter_optimize.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 ┬з6.5 (Optimal runner diameter); Menges 2001 ┬з6.5.

**MOLD-WARPAGE-INDEX** тЬЕ тАФ Heuristic warpage-risk index (0тАУ100) for injection-moulded parts. `compute_warpage_index(WarpageSpec) -> WarpageIndexReport` in `kerf_mold.warpage_index`. Dataclasses: `WarpageSpec` (wall_thickness_uniformity_pct: 0тАУ100, gate_location: "centered"|"edge"|"corner"|"unbalanced", polymer_grade, post_eject_cooling_time_s, mold_temp_C); `WarpageIndexReport` (warpage_index: float, risk_level: "low"|"medium"|"high"|"severe", primary_warp_driver, mitigation_suggestions: list[str], honest_caveat, sub_scores: dict). Scoring (Beaumont 2007 ┬з10 + Menges 2001 ┬з8): wall-uniformity penalty (0тАУ30 pts; piecewise linear: 100%тЖТ0 pts, 80%тЖТ6 pts, 0%тЖТ30 pts); gate-location penalty (0тАУ25 pts: centered=3, edge=14, corner=22, unbalanced=25); polymer grade (0тАУ20 pts: PC=5 low, ABS=7, PP=14 semi-cryst., POM=15, GF-PA66=20 max тАФ Menges 2001 Table 8.2 shrinkage anisotropy); post-eject cooling time (0тАУ15 pts; exponential decay score=15┬╖exp(тИТt/40), characteristic time 40 s per Menges 2001 ┬з8.5 HDT stabilisation); mold temperature deviation from recommended range (0тАУ10 pts). Risk thresholds: 0тАУ24 low, 25тАУ49 medium, 50тАУ74 high, 75тАУ100 severe. Prioritised mitigation suggestions generated per dominant factor. `mold_compute_warpage_index` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 39 tests green. HONEST: heuristic screening tool ONLY (┬▒15 pts uncertainty typical) тАФ real warpage prediction requires full filling + packing + cooling FEM simulation (Moldflow, Moldex3D, SigmaSoft 3D Warp); orientation-dependent shrinkage tensors, part geometry, packing pressure, injection speed, hold time, runner imbalance, sequential valve gating, and residual-stress relaxation are NOT modelled тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/warpage_index.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 ┬з10 (Warpage Analysis); Menges 2001 ┬з8 (Post-mold shrinkage).

**MOLD-COOLING-PRESSURE-DROP** тЬЕ тАФ Total pressure-drop across multi-segment mold cooling-channel networks (Darcy-Weisbach + minor-loss K-factors) + chiller pump head verification. `compute_cooling_pressure_drop(segments, coolant) -> CoolingPressureDropReport` in `kerf_mold.cooling_pressure_drop`. Dataclasses: `CoolingChannelSegment` (length_mm, diameter_mm, segment_type: "straight"|"elbow_90"|"elbow_45"|"tee_thru"|"tee_branch"); `CoolantSpec` (flow_rate_L_per_min, density_kg_m3=1000, viscosity_cP=1.0); `CoolingPressureDropReport` (total_pressure_drop_bar, reynolds_number, friction_factor, segment_breakdown, chiller_head_required_bar, recommended_pump_head_bar, honest_caveat). Algorithm: Re=╧Б┬╖v┬╖D/╬╝; ╬ФP_major=f┬╖(L/D)┬╖(╧Бv┬▓/2); ╬ФP_minor=K┬╖(╧Бv┬▓/2). Smooth-pipe friction: f=64/Re (laminar Re<2300); Blasius f=0.316/Re^0.25 (turbulent Re>4000); linear blend in transition. K-factors: elbow_90=0.9, elbow_45=0.4, tee_thru=0.6, tee_branch=1.8. Recommended pump head=total_╬ФP├Ч1.25 (25% margin). `mold_compute_cooling_pressure_drop` LLM tool registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. HONEST: single-phase incompressible fluid only (water/water-glycol) тАФ no two-phase/boiling flow; no heat-transfer coupling (viscosity spatially uniform); smooth-pipe Blasius only (no Colebrook-White roughness correction); series network assumed (parallel branches need per-branch analysis) тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cooling_pressure_drop.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 ┬з11.2 Table 11.1; White "Fluid Mechanics" 8th ed. ┬з6.7, ┬з6.9.

**ELEC-EMI-FILTER-CUTOFF** тЬЕ тАФ Passive LC/RC power-line EMI filter design per Ott "EMC Engineering" ┬з15.3 + CISPR 22/EN 55022. `design_emi_filter(EmiFilterSpec) -> EmiFilterReport` in `kerf_electronics.emi_filter_design`. Dataclasses: `EmiFilterSpec` (dc_voltage_V, dc_current_A, target_attenuation_dB, target_freq_kHz, filter_topology, load_resistance_ohm=None); `EmiFilterReport` (cutoff_freq_Hz, L_uH, C_uF, R_ohm, attenuation_at_target_dB, recommended_caps_X2_uF, honest_caveat). Three topologies: LC_low_pass (2nd-order тИТ40 dB/dec: f_c = f_t / 10^(A/40), C = 1/((2╧А┬╖f_c)┬▓┬╖L) for L=100 ┬╡H); PI_LC_L (3rd-order ╧А-section тИТ60 dB/dec: f_c = f_t / 10^(A/60), each shunt cap = C/2); RC_low_pass (1st-order тИТ20 dB/dec: f_c = f_t / 10^(A/20), C = 1/(2╧А┬╖f_c┬╖R)). **CAM-TURNING-DEPTH** тЬЕ тАФ Optimal depth-of-cut (DOC) per pass + total roughing passes for a lathe turning operation. `compute_turning_depth(TurningSpec) -> TurningDepthReport` in `kerf_cam.turning_depth_calc`. Dataclasses: `TurningSpec` (stock_diameter_mm, final_diameter_mm, finish_pass_doc_mm=0.5, max_roughing_doc_mm=3.0, material, tool_nose_radius_mm, feed_mm_per_rev, spindle_rpm, workpiece_length_mm=100); `TurningDepthReport` (num_roughing_passes, num_finishing_passes, total_passes, roughing_doc_mm, total_machining_time_s, recommended_doc_for_material, honest_caveat). Material DOC ranges: steel_1018 2тАУ4 mm (rec 3.0), aluminum_6061 4тАУ8 mm (rec 6.0), stainless_303 1.5тАУ2.5 mm (rec 2.0). Refs: MH 31e ┬з1148; Sandvik CoroPlus Turning Catalogue (2024).

**GDT-FEATURE-OF-SIZE-DOF (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬з4.7 + ┬з7.3)** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_fos_dof(FOSSpec) -> FOSDoFReport` enumerates the Degrees of Freedom constrained vs released by a Feature of Size + geometric tolerance combination тАФ critical for inspection planning. Dataclasses: `FOSSpec` (feature_type: "cylinder"|"hole"|"slot"|"sphere"|"planar_pair"|"width", tolerance_symbol: "position"|"perpendicularity"|"parallelism"|"angularity"|"runout"|"total_runout"); `FOSDoFReport` (dof_constrained, dof_released, total_constrained, datum_required_count, code_section, honest_caveat). DOF rules per ┬з4.7 + ┬з7.3: cylinder/hole + position тЖТ TX, TY (axis radial location); cylinder/hole + orientation тЖТ RX, RY (axis tilt); cylinder/hole + runout/total_runout тЖТ TX, TY, RX, RY (┬з7.3.4/┬з7.3.5 coupling); slot/width/planar_pair + position тЖТ TX (centre-plane location); slot + orientation тЖТ RX, RY; sphere + position тЖТ TX, TY, TZ (point location); sphere + orientation тЖТ nothing (rotationally symmetric). `gdt_compute_fos_dof` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 35 tests green. **GDT-RUNOUT-CIRCULAR (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬з12.4)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_circular_runout(CircularRunoutSpec) -> CircularRunoutReport` evaluates single-plane circular runout tolerance compliance per ┬з12.4. Input is structured as a list of cross-section lists тАФ each inner list contains radial measurements at a single axial position (mirrors physical inspection: fixture at zтВА, rotate 360┬░, record N radial readings). Dataclasses: `RunoutMeasurement` (angular_position_deg, radial_measurement_mm, axial_position_mm=0.0); `CircularRunoutSpec` (measurements_per_cross_section: list[list[RunoutMeasurement]], tolerance_mm, datum_axis_id="A"); `CircularRunoutReport` (fim_per_section_mm, max_fim_mm, governing_axial_position_mm, pass_fail: "PASS"|"FAIL", margin_mm, num_measurements_total, honest_caveat). Algorithm (┬з12.4): FIM_s = max(r)тИТmin(r) for each cross-section s; max_FIM = worst section; pass тЯ║ max_FIM тЙд tolerance_mm. margin_mm = tolerance тИТ max_FIM (positive = headroom; negative = overrun). Minimum 3 measurements per section enforced. governing_axial_position_mm identifies the worst-case section; tied FIM тЖТ first section wins. Distinct from runout_check.py (┬з13 point-cloud API): section-oriented input; dedicated ┬з12.4 compliance path; conical surface independence confirmed (per-section FIM=0 when form is perfect even though nominal radius varies axially). Oracle: eccentric cylinder eccentricity=1mm тЖТ FIM=2mm; tol=1mmтЖТFAIL margin=тИТ1mm; tol=2mmтЖТPASS margin=0. `gdt_check_circular_runout` LLM tool registered via gated import; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 27 tests green. HONEST FLAG: measurements must be pre-computed radial distances from the TRUE datum axis; datum simulator computation (minimum zone cylinder тАФ ASME B89.3.1 / ISO 12181-1 ┬з4.3) NOT performed; probe offset/cosine error/thermal corrections must be applied by caller тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/runout_circular.py`.

**GDT-RUNOUT-CHECK (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬з13 + ISO 1101:2017 ┬з18)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_runout(RunoutCheckSpec, list[InspectionPoint]) -> RunoutCheckReport` verifies circular and total runout tolerance compliance for a rotational feature given inspection points measured around a datum axis. Dataclasses: `InspectionPoint` (theta_deg, axial_z_mm, radius_measured_mm); `RunoutCheckSpec` (feature_id, runout_tolerance_mm, runout_type: "circular"|"total", nominal_radius_mm); `RunoutCheckReport` (max_runout_mm, mean_radius_mm, fom, compliant, per_section_runout, honest_caveat). Algorithms per ┬з13: Circular runout (┬з13.2 / ISO ┬з18.3) тАФ group points by axial z-section, runout at each section = max(R)тИТmin(R) = Full Indicator Movement (FIM); max_runout = worst section. Total runout (┬з13.3 / ISO ┬з18.4) тАФ FIM over ALL points simultaneously (max(R)тИТmin(R)); captures taper/coaxiality + form combined; total_runout тЙе circular_runout always. fom = max_runout / tolerance; fom < 1.0 тЖТ pass. Oracle: eccentric cylinder with 0.05 mm axis offset тЖТ circular runout = 2├Ч0.05 = 0.10 mm (2d formula); tapered cylinder (R=10.00тЖТ10.20 mm across 3 z-sections) тЖТ circular_runout=0 per section, total_runout=0.20 mm > circular. `gdt_check_runout` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 26 tests green. HONEST FLAG: ideal datum axis assumed тАФ all radii must be pre-computed from a known datum axis; Chebyshev-optimal (minimum zone) axis fit (ASME B89.3.1 / ISO 12181-1 ┬з4.3) is not performed. Circular runout grouping uses exact z-value equality тАФ real CMM data may require z-binning before calling. Total runout is radial-only (max RтИТmin R); axial deviation for face runout surfaces (ASME ┬з13.3 full definition) is not checked тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/runout_check.py`.

**GDT-DATUM-SHIFT-CHECK (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬з4.5 + ┬з7.3.5)** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_datum_shift(DatumFeatureSpec, base_position_tolerance_mm) -> DatumShiftReport` computes per-datum bonus tolerance (datum shift) when a datum feature of size is referenced with an MMC or LMC modifier in the feature control frame. Dataclasses: `DatumFeatureSpec` (datum_letter, mmc_size_mm, lmc_size_mm, measured_size_mm, material_condition_modifier); `DatumShiftReport` (datum_letter, base_tolerance_zone_mm, bonus_shift_mm, total_available_tolerance_mm, shift_allowed, code_section, honest_caveat). Computation per ┬з4.5 + ┬з7.3.5: MMC modifier тЖТ shift = |measured тИТ MMC|; LMC modifier тЖТ shift = |measured тИТ LMC|; RFS тЖТ shift = 0. **GDT-COMPOSITE-TOLERANCE (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬з10.5.2 + ┬з11.6)** тЬЕ тАФ `validate_composite_frame(CompositeFrameSpec) -> CompositeFrameValidationReport` validates stacked PLTZF/FRTZF composite feature control frames in `kerf_cad_core.gdt.composite_tolerance_check`. Three rules enforced: R1 тАФ all segments share the same geometric symbol (┬з10.5.2(a)); R2 тАФ each lower segment tolerance тЙд segment above it (FRTZF tol тЙд PLTZF tol, ┬з10.5.1 Note 2); R3 тАФ lower segment datum_refs must be a subset of the segment above (┬з10.5.1(b)) тАФ new datums below the PLTZF would imply location constraint, reserved for the PLTZF; FRTZF may only refine orientation. **GDT-COMPOSITE-POSITION (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬з10.5)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_composite_position(CompositePositionSpec) -> CompositePositionReport` evaluates composite positional tolerance compliance for a feature pattern against measured 3-D points. **GDT-DIMENSION-CHAIN (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬з5.3 + Bralla ┬з1)** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_dimension_chain(chain: list[DimensionLink], target_gap_min_mm, target_gap_max_mm) -> DimensionChainReport` computes worst-case (WC) and statistical RSS tolerance stack-up for a linear dimension chain. Dataclasses: `DimensionLink` (link_id, nominal_mm, tol_plus_mm, tol_minus_mm, direction: "positive"|"negative"); `DimensionChainReport` (nominal_gap_mm, worst_case_min_mm, worst_case_max_mm, rss_min_mm, rss_max_mm, links_count, dominant_link, honest_caveat). Algorithm: nominal_gap = ╬г s_i┬╖d_i; WC accumulation T_WC = ╬г max(tтБ║_i, tтБ╗_i); G_wc_min/max = nominal тИУ T_WC; RSS accumulation T_RSS = тИЪ(╬г max(tтБ║_i, tтБ╗_i)┬▓); G_rss_min/max = nominal тИУ T_RSS (3╧Г bilateral, 99.73% assemblability). dominant_link = link with largest half-tolerance. Oracle: +100┬▒0.5 / тИТ30┬▒0.2 / тИТ20┬▒0.1 тЖТ nominal=50 mm; WC=[49.2, 50.8]; RSS=тИЪ0.30=0.5477тЖТ[49.452, 50.548]. `gdt_compute_dimension_chain` LLM tool registered via gated import pattern; registered in plugin.py `_TOOL_MODULES`; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.gdt`. 24 tests green. HONEST FLAG: RSS assumes independent, normally distributed component dimensions centred on nominal (Cpk=1.0 for all links); correlation between links (e.g. same fixture datum) and non-normal distributions are not modelled тАФ RSS is unconservative in those cases; Monte Carlo with measured process distributions is more accurate per Bralla ┬з1 тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/gdt/dimension_chain.py`. Refs: ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬з5.3; Bralla "Design for Manufacturability Handbook" ┬з1.

**GK-P13 SUBD-G1-EXTRAORDINARY-PATCHES** тЬЕ тАФ G1 continuity at extraordinary-vertex SubDтЖТNURBS patch conversion. `convert_subd_to_g1_patches(spec: ExtraordinaryPatchSpec) -> G1PatchResult` builds n bicubic B├йzier patches around a Catmull-Clark extraordinary vertex (valence n тЙа 4) with Loop (1987) ┬з4 tangent-plane continuity enforcement: (1) apply `num_iterations` CC subdivisions to isolate the EV; (2) compute EV limit position V_inf via Stam (1998) ┬з3.1; (3) build n 4├Ч4 B├йzier CP grids in the Stam limit-tangent plane, one per face sector; (4) project second-row CPs of adjacent patches into the Stam tangent plane at V_inf to enforce G1 across all n shared boundary edges. Dataclasses: `ExtraordinaryPatchSpec` (cage_mesh: SubdCage, extraordinary_vertex_idx: int, num_iterations: int=2); `G1PatchResult` (n_patches int = valence, patch_control_points_per_patch: list[list[list[tuple]]] 4├Ч4 CP grid per patch, max_g1_residual_deg: float, mean_g1_residual_deg: float, valence: int, honest_caveat: str). G1 residual measured as inter-patch normal angle (degrees, sampled at 5 points per shared edge). LLM tool `subd_convert_to_g1_patches` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 32 oracle-asserted tests green (valence-3 cube corner 3 patches + G1 residual < 1┬░, valence-5 dome EV 5 patches + G1 < 1┬░, valence-4 regular warns + 4 patches, valence-6 hex EV 6 patches, out-of-range idx returns empty, zero iterations runs, re-export from subd package, honest_caveat mentions Loop/G1/Peters-Reif, multiple subdivision levels 1-3 finite residuals, n_patches==valence invariant). HONEST: Loop (1987) G1 construction only тАФ Peters-Reif G2 (curvature continuity) NOT implemented (requires degree тЙе 5 patches, Peters-Reif 2008 ┬з7.4); high-valence EVs (n тЙе 8) may show curvature inflation due to convex-hull property of bicubic B├йzier patches; G1 residual < 1┬░ achieved for n=3,5 test cases. Refs: Loop (1987) MS Thesis ┬з4 Utah; Stam (1998) ┬з3.1тАУ3.3 SIGGRAPH; Peters-Reif (2008) Subdivision Surfaces ┬з7.4; Reif (1995) CAGD 12(2) тАФ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/g1_extraordinary_patches.py`.

**GK-P12 SUBD-STAM-LIMIT-TANGENTS** тЬЕ тАФ exact limit tangent vectors at extraordinary Catmull-Clark SubD vertices (valence n тЙа 4) using the eigenstructure decomposition from Stam (1998) ┬з3.2тАУ3.3. `compute_stam_limit_tangents(ev: ExtraordinaryVertex, ring_positions=None) -> LimitTangentReport` computes: V_inf = w_V┬╖V + w_e┬╖╬гP_i + w_f┬╖╬гQ_i (limit position, Stam ┬з3.2 eq. 3.1); T_u = ╬г cos(2╧Аi/n)┬╖(P_i тИТ V_inf); T_v = ╬г sin(2╧Аi/n)┬╖(P_i тИТ V_inf) (limit tangents, Stam ┬з3.3); N = T_u ├Ч T_v (unit normal, C┬╣-continuous at EV per Reif 1995); subdominant eigenvalue ╬╗_n = (1/4)(1 + cos(2╧А/n)); approximate Gaussian curvature K (angle-deficit / Gauss-Bonnet, Meyer et al. 2003 ┬з4) and mean curvature H (cotangent-weight Laplace-Beltrami, Meyer et al. 2003 ┬з3.3). Dataclasses: `ExtraordinaryVertex` (vertex_index, valence, position_xyz_mm, one_ring_vertices, one_ring_faces); `LimitTangentReport` (tangent_u, tangent_v, normal_xyz, gaussian_curvature_estimate, mean_curvature_estimate, valence, eigenvalue_subdominant, honest_caveat). LLM tool `subd_compute_stam_limit_tangents` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 30 oracle-asserted tests green (regular v4 flat normal Z, flat T_u/T_v in XY, flat KтЙИ0, flat HтЙИ0, unit normal all valences, nonzero tangent magnitudes, dome v3/5/6 K>0, dome normal outward, hex v6 symmetric tangent magnitudes, eigenvalue formula for v3/4/6/5/7, limit weights partition-of-unity all n, reexport from subd package, tangents span plane, synthetic fallback no crash, honest caveat non-empty + "Stam"). DISTINCT from `limit_normal_fit.py` (which samples face grids) тАФ this is the closed-form Stam formula AT the extraordinary vertex point itself. HONEST: tangent vectors EXACT per Stam ┬з3.3; curvature estimates APPROXIMATE (discrete polyhedral estimators, CC surface is only C┬╣ at EV so C┬▓-based curvature has limited meaning); distinct from the face-sampling `limit_normal_fit.py` тАФ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/stam_limit_tangents.py`. Refs: Stam (1998) ┬з3.2тАУ3.3 SIGGRAPH; Reif (1995) CAGD 12(2); Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD ┬з10(6); Meyer et al. (2003) "Discrete Differential-Geometry Operators for Triangulated 2-Manifolds" ┬з3тАУ4.

**GK-P19 SUBD-FEATURE-CURVES** тЬЕ тАФ extract characteristic "ridge" and "valley" polylines from a Catmull-Clark SubD limit surface (or refined cage) using discrete principal-curvature analysis. `extract_feature_curves(spec: FeatureCurveSpec) -> FeatureCurveResult` subdivides the cage `subdivision_level` times (Catmull-Clark 1978), estimates per-vertex normals (area-weighted face normals), computes Taubin (1995) curvature tensor at each vertex (edge normal-curvature accumulation тЖТ 3├Ч3 tensor projected to tangent plane тЖТ eigenvalues ╬║тВБ тЙе ╬║тВВ), then classifies vertices as ridge (╬║тВБ > ridge_threshold_per_mm) or valley (╬║тВВ < тИТvalley_threshold_per_mm) and chains them into polylines via BFS edge-following. Dataclasses: `FeatureCurveSpec` (cage: SubdCage, subdivision_level: int=2, ridge_threshold_per_mm: float=0.1, valley_threshold_per_mm: float=0.1); `FeatureCurve` (kind: str "ridge"|"valley", polyline_xyz_mm: list[tuple], length_mm: float, mean_principal_curvature: float); `FeatureCurveResult` (curves, num_ridges, num_valleys, total_ridge_length_mm, total_valley_length_mm, max_principal_curvature, honest_caveat). LLM tool `subd_extract_feature_curves` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 26 oracle-asserted tests green (flat plane 0 ridges + 0 valleys, flat plane max ╬║тВБ near zero, cube cage ridges detected + positive curvature + finite coords, saddle cage features detected, sphere high threshold = 0 ridges, API contracts тАФ empty cage, spec/dataclass defaults, kindтИИ{ridge,valley}, threshold monotonicity, re-export). Use cases: ZBrush-style topology hints; automatic UV-seam generation along high-curvature lines; feature detection for re-meshing or CAM path planning. HONEST CAVEATS: DISCRETE CURVATURE APPROXIMATION тАФ principal curvatures via discrete cotangent Laplacian (Meyer et al. 2003), NOT exact CC limit-surface evaluation; errors O(h┬▓) in edge length; sufficient for UV-seam/topology hints but NOT precision curvature analysis. THRESHOLD TUNING тАФ ridge/valley thresholds are scale-dependent (mmтБ╗┬╣); defaults (0.1 mmтБ╗┬╣) are a starting point, retune for your object scale. PERFORMANCE тАФ vertex count scales O(4^L) with subdivision_level L. Refs: Ohtake, Belyaev & Seidel (2004) "Ridge-Valley Lines on Meshes via Implicit Surface Fitting" SIGGRAPH; Meyer et al. (2003) "Discrete Differential-Geometry Operators for Triangulated 2-Manifolds" VisMath; Taubin (1995) "Estimating the Tensor of Curvature of a Surface" ICCV; Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD 10(6); Stam (1998) SIGGRAPH; OpenSubdiv docs тАФ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/feature_curves.py`.

**GK-P14 SUBD-CREASE-FRACTIONAL-DECAY** тЬЕ тАФ semi-sharp fractional crease multi-level decay for Catmull-Clark SubD. `apply_fractional_crease_decay(spec: FractionalCreaseSpec) -> CreaseDecayResult` applies the DeRose-Kass-Truong (1998) ┬з4 rule: s_new = max(0, s_old тИТ 1) per subdivision level. After L levels: s_L = max(0, sтВА тИТ L). Dataclasses: `CreasedEdge` (v0_idx, v1_idx, sharpness тИИ [0,тИЮ)); `FractionalCreaseSpec` (cage: SubdCage, edges: list[CreasedEdge], subdivision_level: int); `CreaseDecayResult` (decayed_edges: list[CreasedEdge], effective_dihedral_smoothing_per_edge: list[float] 0=fully sharp/1=fully smooth, max_sharpness_remaining: float, num_fully_decayed: int, honest_caveat: str). Smooth-weight formula: smooth_weight = 1 тИТ clamp(s_L, 0, 1) тАФ matches OpenSubdiv fractional crease blend definition. Convention: s тЙе 10 тЙИ permanently sharp (OpenSubdiv). LLM tool `subd_apply_crease_decay` registered in plugin.py via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`. 42 oracle-asserted tests green (infinite s=100 sharp at all levels, s=2 at L=0/1/2/3, s=0.5 half-sharp then smooth, mixed crease set 4 edges, monotonic increasing smooth_weight, empty edge list, level-0 identity, re-export from subd init, honest caveat non-empty + mentions schedule-only + DeRose, OpenSubdiv s=10 convention at L=9/L=10, negative sharpness clamped, large level clamps to zero, never negative). HONEST: SHARPNESS SCHEDULE ONLY тАФ applies the s-1 rule per level and returns decayed s-values + blend weights; does NOT simulate the resulting subdivided cage geometry, does NOT apply CC face/edge/vertex splitting operators; cage vertices/faces passed through unchanged; blended mesh evaluation (interpolating between smooth and sharp CC rules for sтИИ(0,1)) is out of scope тАФ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/crease_fractional_decay.py`. Refs: DeRose-Kass-Truong (1998) ┬з4 SIGGRAPH; OpenSubdiv Subdivision Surfaces docs; Catmull-Clark (1978) CAD 10(6).

**SUBD-LIMIT-NORMAL-FIT** тЬЕ тАФ sample the Catmull-Clark limit-surface normal n╠В(u,v) at a uniform (u,v) grid across all cage faces using Stam (1998) exact eigenstructure tangent vectors; `sample_subd_limit_normals(cage_mesh, samples_per_face=9, normalize=True)` returns `LimitNormalFitResult(sampled_normals, max_normal_residual_deg, mean_normal_residual_deg, num_irregular_samples, honest_caveat)`; per-face n├Чn grid (n = round(sqrt(samples_per_face))); normal via N = тИВS/тИВu ├Ч тИВS/тИВv from Stam tangents (C┬╣-continuous at extraordinary vertices, exact bi-cubic B-spline for valence-4 regular faces); residuals computed against bilinear interpolation of four face-corner Stam normals тАФ quantifies accuracy gain of a proper normal field vs the simple shader approximation; irregular-vertex flag per sample (valence тЙа 4 faces); LLM tool `subd_sample_limit_normals` registered in plugin via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core.subd`; 17 oracle-asserted tests (flat plane nz > 0.9999, unit-length all faces, nx/ny тЙИ 0, dot > 0.9999, normalize=True/False, result structure, total sample count, honest_caveat non-empty, irregular cube valence-3 > 0, flat plane residual < 0.5┬░, max residual тЙд 90┬░, cylinder normals perpendicular to Y, cube 24-sample count + unit-length, empty cage no exception). HONEST: "fit" = residual analysis vs bilinear, NOT a closed-form NURBS surface (would require overdetermined least-squares + knot/CP storage) тАФ `kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/subd/limit_normal_fit.py`. Refs: Stam (1998) ┬з3.2; Halstead-Kass-DeRose (1993); Piegl-Tiller ┬з9.

**ARCH-BASE-PLATE-AISC (AISC DG-1 ┬з3.1 + AISC 360-22 ┬зJ8)** тЬЕ тАФ `design_base_plate(ColumnSpec, ConcreteSpec, Fy=345.0) -> BasePlateReport` implements steel column base plate design for concentric axial compressive loads. Concrete bearing strength: Pp = 0.85┬╖f'c┬╖A1┬╖тИЪ(A2/A1) with A2/A1 тЙд 4 (AISC 360-22 ┬зJ8 Eq J8-2); ╧Ж_c = 0.65; required A1 = P_u/(╧Ж_c┬╖0.85┬╖f'c┬╖тИЪ(A2/A1)). Plate dimensions rounded up to nearest 5 mm; must cover column footprint (0.95┬╖d ├Ч 0.80┬╖bf per DG-1 ┬з3.1.1). Cantilever arms: m=(NтИТ0.95┬╖d)/2 (Eq 3.1-1); n=(BтИТ0.80┬╖bf)/2 (Eq 3.1-2); n'=тИЪ(d┬╖bf)/4; X=[4┬╖d┬╖bf/(d+bf)┬▓]┬╖[P_u/(╧Ж_c┬╖Pp)] (Eq 3.1-8); ╬╗=min(1, 2┬╖тИЪX/(1+тИЪ(1тИТX))); l=max(m,n,╬╗┬╖n'). Plate thickness via Murray-Stockwell (DG-1 Eq 3.1-5): t=l┬╖тИЪ(2┬╖P_u/(0.9┬╖Fy┬╖B┬╖N)), rounded up to 1 mm. Oracle: W14x90, P=1000 kN, f'c=30 MPa, ped 600├Ч600 mm тЖТ A1_reqтЙИ30166 mm┬▓; plate 295├Ч340 mm (column footprint governs, N_min=338 mm, B_min=295 mm); t=15 mm; DCR=0.318 (adequate). `arch_design_base_plate` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import). Re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 24 hermetic oracle tests pass тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/base_plate_aisc.py`. *SCOPE: concentric axial compressive load ONLY (DG-1 ┬з3.1). NOT covered: moment transfer (DG-1 ┬з3.2), anchor rod design (DG-1 ┬з3.3тАУ3.4), shear lug (DG-1 ┬з3.5), biaxial bending, tensile uplift. A2 taken as pedestal plan area; irregular pedestals must supply equivalent rectangular A2. Grout strength тЙе f'c assumed.*

**ARCH-BEAM-DEFLECTION (Roark 9e ┬з8 + AISC Manual Table 3-23)** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_beam_deflection(BeamSpec) -> BeamDeflectionReport` implements five closed-form Euler-Bernoulli beam cases: (1) simply_supported + point_center: ╬┤=PL┬│/(48EI), M=PL/4 [Roark Table 8.1 case 7; AISC 3-23 diag 1]; (2) simply_supported + udl: ╬┤=5wLтБ┤/(384EI), M=wL┬▓/8 [case 2; diag 2]; (3) cantilever + point_center (tip load): ╬┤=PL┬│/(3EI), M=PL [case 1; diag 6]; (4) cantilever + udl: ╬┤=wLтБ┤/(8EI), M=wL┬▓/2 [case 3; diag 7]; (5) fixed_fixed + udl: ╬┤=wLтБ┤/(384EI), M=wL┬▓/12 [case 15; diag 9]. `BeamDeflectionReport` returns ╬┤_max_mm, M_max_Nmm, V_max_N, deflection_location_mm, honest_caveat. `arch_compute_beam_deflection` LLM tool registered in plugin; gated import (registry unavailable тЖТ module still importable). 39 hermetic oracle tests pass (formula verification тЙд0.1%; W14x90 L=6 m P=100 kN ╬┤тЙИ5.41 mm hand-verified; zero-loadтЖТzero; fixed_fixed+point_center тЖТ ValueError; invalid inputs тЖТ ValueError; re-export from arch/__init__.py) тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/beam_deflection.py`. *Scope: linear-elastic, small-deflection Euler-Bernoulli only. No shear deformation (Timoshenko), no lateral-torsional buckling, no yield check, no partial-span loads.*

**ARCH-COLUMN-LOAD-CHECK (AISC 360-22 ┬зE3 + ACI 318-19 ┬з22.4)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_steel_column(SteelColumnSpec, P_kN) -> ColumnLoadReport` implements AISC 360-22 ┬зE3 LRFD: Fe = ╧А┬▓E/(KL/r)┬▓, inelastic Fcr = 0.658^(Fy/Fe)┬╖Fy (E3-2) for KL/r тЙд 4.71тИЪ(E/Fy), elastic Fcr = 0.877┬╖Fe (E3-3) otherwise, ╧Ж_c = 0.90, slender-column flag at KL/r > 200. `check_concrete_column(ConcreteColumnSpec, P_kN) -> ColumnLoadReport` implements ACI 318-19 ┬з22.4.2.2: ╧Ж┬╖Pn = ╧Ж┬╖0.80┬╖[0.85┬╖f'c┬╖(AgтИТAst) + fy┬╖Ast], ╧Ж = 0.65 tied (0.75 spiral), ╧Бg bounds check per ┬з10.6.1.1. **ARCH-FOOTING-BEARING-CAPACITY (Meyerhof 1963 / Bowles 5e ┬з4 / Das 8e ┬з3)** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_bearing_capacity(FootingSpec, SoilProperties, FS=3.0) -> BearingCapacityReport` implements the Meyerhof (1963) general bearing capacity equation q_ult = c┬╖N_c┬╖s_c┬╖d_c + ╬│┬╖Df┬╖N_q┬╖s_q┬╖d_q + 0.5┬╖╬│┬╖B┬╖N_╬│┬╖s_╬│┬╖d_╬│ for shallow footings on cohesive/cohesionless soil. N-factors: N_q = e^(╧А┬╖tan╧Ж)┬╖tan┬▓(45+╧Ж/2); N_c = (N_qтИТ1)┬╖cot╧Ж (╧Ж=0: N_c=5.14 Prandtl limit); N_╬│ = (N_qтИТ1)┬╖tan(1.4╧Ж). Shape factors s_c, s_q, s_╬│ per Bowles Table 4-4 for strip/square/circular/rectangular. Depth factors d_c, d_q, d_╬│ per Bowles Table 4-4. q_allow = q_ult / FS (default 3.0). `BearingCapacityReport` returns q_ult_kPa, q_allow_kPa, FS, N_c/N_q/N_╬│, s_c, d_c, honest_caveat. `arch_compute_bearing_capacity` LLM tool registered in plugin; gated import pattern. 25 hermetic oracle tests pass (╧Ж=30┬░: N_c=30.14, N_q=18.40, N_╬│=15.67 within 1%; ╧Ж=0 clay 50 kPa square 2├Ч2m Df=1m formula verified q_ult=357.24 kPa; strip s=1; square s>1; depth factors increase with Df/B; custom FS; rectangular interpolation; ValueError on bad inputs; re-export from arch/__init__.py) тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/footing_bearing.py`. *Scope: Meyerhof (1963) shape+depth factors only. No Brinch Hansen rigidity index (I_r) correction, no inclined/eccentric loads, no seismic, no liquefaction, no layered-soil punching-shear.*

**ARCH-SLAB-DEFLECTION (Timoshenko ┬з44 Tables 41тАУ42 + Roark 9e Table 11.4)** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_slab_deflection(SlabSpec, LoadSpec) -> SlabDeflectionReport` implements closed-form center-point deflection for two-way rectangular slabs under uniform load via Kirchhoff thin-plate theory: ╬┤_max = ╬▒┬╖q┬╖aтБ┤/D; D = E┬╖h┬│/(12┬╖(1тИТ╬╜┬▓)). Moment outputs: M_xx = ╬▓_x┬╖q┬╖a┬▓, M_yy = ╬▓_y┬╖q┬╖a┬▓ (Timoshenko Table 41 ╬▓ coefficients). `SlabDeflectionReport` returns delta_max_mm, M_max_xx_Nmm_per_mm, M_max_yy_Nmm_per_mm, plate_stiffness_D, honest_caveat. `arch_compute_slab_deflection` LLM tool registered in plugin; gated import pattern (registry unavailable тЖТ still importable). 21 hermetic oracle tests pass (╬▒=0.00406 within 1%; a/b=2 ╬▒=0.01013; a/b=1.5 ╬▒=0.00772; h┬│ stiffness scaling; load linearity; FF < SS ╬┤; FF ╬▒=0.00126; zero load тЖТ zero; D exact; one-way limit; MтЙе0; all 6 validation error paths; re-export; dimension-order symmetry) тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/slab_deflection.py`. *Scope: linear-elastic Kirchhoff thin plate only. NOT included: shear deformation (Mindlin тАФ significant for h/a > ~0.1); plastic hinge redistribution; concrete cracking / tension stiffening; creep / shrinkage; orthotropic / ribbed slabs; punching shear; exact Timoshenko double-series for intermediate fixed-fixed a/b ratios.*

**ARCH-SLAB-ON-GRADE (ACI 360R-10 + PCA EB119 + Westergaard 1948)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_slab_on_grade(SlabOnGradeSpec) -> SlabOnGradeReport` checks unreinforced concrete slab-on-grade thickness adequacy under a concentrated interior point/wheel load. **ARCH-OPENING-IN-WALL (IBC ┬з2308.4 + ACI 318-19 ┬з11.5.3.1 + TMS 402-22 ┬з5/┬з8.3)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_opening(WallOpeningSpec) -> OpeningCheckReport` checks a wall opening (door/window) for code-compliant tributary load redistribution to jamb piers and lintel/header adequacy. Tributary width per jamb (IBC ┬з2308.4 prescriptive intent): trib_w = opening_width/2 + jamb_width/2 + header_above_opening_height. Jamb capacity: concrete тЖТ ACI 318-19 ┬з11.5.3.1 empirical (╧Ж=0.65, k=1.0 pin-pin): ╧Ж┬╖Pn = 0.55┬╖╧Ж┬╖f'c┬╖Ag┬╖[1тИТ(h/(32t))┬▓]; masonry тЖТ TMS 402-22 ┬з8.3 Eq 8-22 (╧Ж=0.60): r=t/тИЪ12, C_s=1тИТ(h_eff/(140r))┬▓, ╧Ж┬╖Pn=╧Ж┬╖0.80┬╖f'm┬╖Ag┬╖C_s; wood_frame тЖТ simplified bearing ╧Ж┬╖Pn=╧Ж┬╖Fc┬╖Ag (NDS Cp NOT computed). Oracle (concrete, 3m wall, 200mm thick, 1.2m├Ч1.5m window, fc=30MPa, jamb=0.4m, axial=30kN/m, lateral=1.0kN/m┬▓): trib_w=1.8m, Pu=65.7kN, ╧Ж┬╖PnтЙИ812kN, jamb DCRтЙИ0.081; all_adequate=True. `OpeningCheckReport` returns tributary_load_on_jamb_kN, jamb_axial_capacity_kN, jamb_dcr, lintel_moment_dcr, lintel_deflection_mm, all_adequate, governing_check, honest_caveat. `arch_check_opening_in_wall` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import); re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 25 hermetic oracle tests pass тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/opening_in_wall.py`. *SCOPE: SIMPLIFIED TRIBUTARY METHOD тАФ full 2-D FE stress-concentration analysis around opening corners NOT modelled (St. Venant diffusion тЙИ 1тАУ2├Ч opening dimension; may be unconservative for wide openings > wall_height/2 or clustered openings). Jamb: ACI ┬з11.5.3.1 empirical formula only тАФ small eccentricity (eтЙИ0) assumed; large eccentricity requires PM interaction (ACI ┬з11.4). Wood-frame: NDS 2018 Cp NOT computed. **ARCH-LINTEL-DESIGN (AISC Manual Table 3-23 + ACI 318-19 ┬з9 + TMS 402-22 ┬з5)** тЬЕ тАФ `design_lintel(LintelSpec) -> LintelDesignReport` checks steel, reinforced-concrete, and reinforced-masonry lintels over wall openings for moment, shear, and deflection. Steel capacity (rectangular section approx): ╧Ж┬╖Mn = 0.90┬╖Fy┬╖S_x; ╧Ж┬╖Vn = 1.00┬╖0.6┬╖Fy┬╖0.5┬╖b┬╖h (╧Ж_b=0.90, ╧Ж_v=1.00, AISC 360-22 ┬зF1/┬зG2.1). **ARCH-BEARING-WALL-AXIAL (ACI 318-19 ┬з11.5.3.1 + TMS 402-22 ┬з8.3 + Wight ┬з13.13)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_bearing_wall(BearingWallSpec, P_factored_kN_per_m, phi=0.65) -> BearingWallReport` implements axial-load capacity of plain concrete, reinforced concrete, and masonry bearing walls (unit-strip per metre width). **ARCH-PIER-AXIAL (TMS 402-22 ┬з8.3 + ACI 318-19 ┬з22.4.2.2 + Drysdale-Hamid ┬з10)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_pier_axial(PierSpec, P_factored_kN, phi=0.65) -> PierAxialReport` implements axial-load capacity of slender masonry and reinforced concrete piers with TMS Eq 8-22 h/r slenderness reduction. Slenderness factor: C_s = 1 тИТ (h_eff/(140┬╖r))┬▓ (TMS Eq 8-22), valid for h_eff/r тЙд 99; h_eff/r > 99 тЖТ slenderness_limit_exceeded (╧Ж┬╖Pn = 0). Effective height: h_eff = k┬╖h per end_conditions тАФ fixed_fixed k=0.5, pin_pin k=1.0, fixed_pin k=0.7, cantilever k=2.0 (Drysdale-Hamid ┬з10). `PierAxialReport` returns phi_Pn_kN, slenderness_factor, h_over_r, governing_failure_mode (yielding|slender_buckling|slenderness_limit_exceeded), honest_caveat. Oracle (200├Ч200mm pin-pin h=3000mm clay_masonry f'm=10MPa): r=57.7mm, h/r=52.0, C_s=1тИТ(3000/(140├Ч57.7))┬▓тЙИ0.862, ╧Ж┬╖PnтЙИ179.5 kN; h/r>99 (e.g. h=6000mm pin-pin) тЖТ slenderness_limit_exceeded; fixed_fixed тЖТ smaller h_eff тЖТ larger C_s; RC path verifies ACI ┬з22.4.2.2 contribution. `arch_check_pier_axial` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import); re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 49 hermetic oracle tests pass тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/pier_axial_capacity.py`. *SCOPE: Concentric axial load ONLY тАФ eccentricity, moment interaction (PM curve), and combined axial+bending NOT modelled. **ARCH-RETAINING-WALL-STABILITY (Bowles 5e ┬з12.3 + Das ┬з13 тАФ Rankine active)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_retaining_wall(RetainingWallSpec, SoilSpec) -> RetainingWallReport` implements overturning, sliding, and bearing stability checks for cantilevered concrete retaining walls under Rankine active earth pressure. Ka = tan┬▓(45тИТ╧Ж/2); Pa = 0.5┬╖╬│_s┬╖H┬▓┬╖Ka (horizontal resultant, at H/3). Weight components per metre: W_stem = ╬│_c┬╖t┬╖(HтИТh); W_base = ╬│_c┬╖B┬╖h; W_soil = ╬│_s┬╖l_heel┬╖(HтИТh). Moments about toe: M_resist = W_stem┬╖(l_toe+t/2) + W_base┬╖(B/2) + W_soil┬╖(BтИТl_heel/2); M_overt = Pa┬╖(H/3). FoS_overturning = M_resist/M_overt (min 2.0). FoS_sliding = ╬гW┬╖tan(╬┤)/Pa (min 1.5). Bearing: e = B/2 тИТ (M_resistтИТM_overt)/╬гW; q_max = (╬гW/B)┬╖(1+6e/B) (trapezoidal; triangular when e>B/6); FoS_bearing = q_a/q_max (min 3.0). `RetainingWallReport` returns Ka, Pa_kN_per_m, FoS_overturning, FoS_sliding, q_max_kPa, FoS_bearing, all_adequate, governing_failure_mode, honest_caveat. Oracle (H=3m, B=2m, t=0.3m, h=0.3m, l_heel=1.5m, l_toe=0.2m, ╬│_c=24, ╬│_s=18, ╧Ж=30┬░): Ka=1/3, Pa=27.0 kN/m, FoS_overt=4.16 (adequate), FoS_sliding=1.44 (inadequate at ╬┤=20┬░; adequate at ╬┤=25┬░). `arch_check_retaining_wall_stability` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import); re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 27 hermetic oracle tests pass тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/retaining_wall_stability.py`. *SCOPE: Rankine ACTIVE pressure only тАФ level backfill, cohesionless (c=0). NO surcharge load. NO seismic (Mononobe-Okabe, AASHTO LRFD ┬з11.6.5 / Das ┬з13.12). NO passive resistance from toe soil (conservative). NO hydrostatic pressure (free-draining assumed). Bearing: trapezoidal pressure distribution; triangular applied automatically for e>B/6. Always verify with a licensed geotechnical/structural engineer.*

**ARCH-SHEAR-WALL-OOP (ACI 318-19 ┬з11.7 + ┬з22.3 + Wight ┬з13.13)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_shear_wall_oop(ShearWallSpec, phi=0.65) -> ShearWallOOPReport` implements out-of-plane (OOP) flexural capacity check for RC shear walls under combined axial + lateral (wind/seismic) loads. **ARCH-PUNCHING-SHEAR (ACI 318-19 ┬з22.6 + Wight ┬з13.10)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_punching_shear(ColumnSlabSpec, V_applied_kN, phi=0.75) -> PunchingShearReport` implements two-way (punching) shear capacity check for flat concrete slabs around columns per ACI 318-19 ┬з22.6. **ARCH-LATERAL-BRACING (AISC 360-22 ┬зF2 + AISC Manual Table 3-2)** тЬЕ тАФ `check_lateral_bracing(WSectionSpec, L_b_mm, Cb=1.0) -> LateralBracingReport` implements AISC 360-22 ┬зF2 LRFD for compact doubly symmetric I-shaped members bent about the major axis. Equations: Lp = 1.76┬╖ry┬╖тИЪ(E/Fy) (F2-5); Lr = 1.95┬╖rts┬╖(E/0.7Fy)┬╖тИЪ(Jc/Sxho + тИЪ((Jc/Sxho)┬▓+6.76┬╖(0.7Fy/E)┬▓)) (F2-6); Zone 1 LbтЙдLp тЖТ Mn = Mp = Fy┬╖Zx (F2-1, yielding); Zone 2 Lp<LbтЙдLr тЖТ Mn = Cb┬╖[MpтИТ(MpтИТ0.7┬╖Fy┬╖Sx)┬╖(LbтИТLp)/(LrтИТLp)]тЙдMp (F2-2, inelastic_LTB); Zone 3 Lb>Lr тЖТ Mn = Fcr┬╖SxтЙдMp, Fcr = Cb┬╖╧А┬▓E/(Lb/rts)┬▓┬╖тИЪ(1+0.078┬╖Jc/(Sx┬╖ho)┬╖(Lb/rts)┬▓) (F2-3/4, elastic_LTB). ╧Ж_b = 0.90; c=1.0 (F2-8a). `LateralBracingReport` returns Lp, Lr, Mp, Mr, Mn, phi_Mn, governing_mode ("yielding"|"inelastic_LTB"|"elastic_LTB"), Lb_to_Lp_ratio, honest_caveat. W14x90 oracle (Fy=345 MPa): Lp=3 983 mm (тЙИ4.0 m), Lr=12 962 mm (тЙИ13.0 m), Mp=887.6 kN┬╖m, Mr=565.9 kN┬╖m тАФ consistent with AISC Manual Table 3-2. `arch_check_lateral_bracing` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import). 27 hermetic tests pass тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/lateral_bracing_check.py`. *SCOPE: doubly symmetric compact I-shaped members (W-shapes) ONLY. Channels (┬зF6), tees (┬зF9), single angles (┬зF10), and built-up sections (┬зF4/F5) are out of scope. Compact section assumed тАФ bf/(2┬╖tf) and h/tw flange/web compactness NOT verified here. Cb must be supplied by caller; not computed from moment diagram.*

**GDT-DATUM-PRECEDENCE-WARN (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬з4.7 + ┬з4.11)** тЬЕ тАФ `analyze_datum_precedence_consistency(frames, datums) -> PrecedenceReport` checks a set of feature control frames for cross-frame datum inconsistencies: P1 feature-type conflict (same datum letter as planar in one frame, FOS in another тАФ ERROR); P1b datum at multiple precedence levels тАФ WARNING; P2 precedence reversal (A|B|C vs B|A|C тАФ WARNING, ┬з4.11); P3 DOF over-constraint (>6 DOF from declared datum sequence тАФ ERROR, ┬з4.7); P4 modifier conflict (RMB vs MMB vs LMB on same datum тАФ WARNING, ┬з4.11.5). `PrecedenceReport` dataclass: `warnings`, `consistent`, `frames_analysed`, `recommendations`. Each `PrecedenceWarning`: `code`, `severity` (ERROR/WARNING), `message`, `rule`, `affected_frames`, `datum_label`, `recommendation`. `gdt_warn_datum_precedence` LLM tool registered. DOF budget per ┬з4.7: planar primary=3, cylinder primary=2, sphere primary=3, planar secondary=2, FOS secondary=1, tertiary=1. HONEST FLAG: analyses declared datum properties only тАФ geometric consistency requires the solid model. Oracles: Fig. 4-1 (3-2-1 planar тЖТ clean); Fig. 4-2 (FOS cylinder primary RMB тЖТ clean); ┬з4.11 text (A|B|C vs B|A|C тЖТ PRECEDENCE_REVERSAL). 41 tests тАФ `packages/kerf-gdnt/src/kerf_gdnt/datum_precedence_warn.py`.

### Latest delta тАФ 2026-05-30

**GD&T composite tolerance frame (ASME Y14.5-2018 ┬з10.5)** тЬЕ тАФ `parse_composite_frame(text)` + `validate_composite_frame(frame)` implement full ┬з10.5 PLTZF/FRTZF validation: R2 FRTZF tolerance тЙд PLTZF tolerance (┬з10.5.1 Note 2); R3 FRTZF primary datum must match PLTZF primary (┬з10.5.1(a)); R4 FRTZF datums must be a precedence-ordered subset of PLTZF datums, no new datums (┬з10.5.1(b)); R5 symbol must match between lines. `gdt_validate_composite_tolerance_frame` LLM tool registered. **BREP-SOLID-CONTAINS-POINT** тЬЕ тАФ Ray-casting Jordan-curve inside/outside test for B-rep solids: `solid_contains_point(body, point, tolerance=1e-6) -> ContainmentResult` casts a generic-direction ray (1, 0.013, 0.029) from the query point and counts boundary crossings; odd = inside, even = outside. `ContainmentResult` dataclass: `inside` (bool|None), `on_boundary`, `ray_hits`, `degenerate_ray`. Planar faces use exact ray-polygon (loop vertices); analytic/NURBS faces use UV-grid triangulation (M├╢ller-Trumbore per triangle, default 32├Ч32 grid). Degenerate-ray honest flag: if primary direction is parallel to a face, fallback direction (0.017, 1, 0.011) is tried; if both disagree on parity, `degenerate_ray=True` and `inside=None`. LLM tool `brep_solid_contains_point` registered. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. Oracles: cube interior/exterior/boundary; sphere interior/exterior/near-boundary/boundary; torus tube-interior/hole-outside/boundary; L-shape concave notch; 25 tests green. Refs: Mortenson ┬з11.5; Ericson 2005 ┬з5.1; O'Rourke ┬з7.4 тАФ `kerf-cad-core/geom/solid_contains_point.py`.
### Latest delta тАФ 2026-05-31

**NURBS-CURVE-FRESNEL-PARAMETERIZE** тЬЕ тАФ `fresnel_parameterize_curve(curve, num_samples=200, target_kappa_rate=1.0)` returns `FresnelParameterizationResult(curve_out, max_curvature_residual, fresnel_S, fresnel_C, honest_caveat)`; re-parameterizes a NurbsCurve so that curvature grows linearly with arc-length (╬║(s) тЙИ ╬▒┬╖s тАФ Euler spiral / clothoid / Cornu spiral law). Algorithm: (1) arc-lengthтАУuniform sampling via adaptive 5-pt Gauss-Legendre; (2) Fresnel integral evaluation C(╧Г), S(╧Г) with ╧Г=s┬╖тИЪ(╬▒/╧А) (Abramowitz-Stegun ┬з7.3); (3) monotone Fresnel-C parameter sequence drives NURBS re-interpolation (Piegl-Tiller ┬з9.2); (4) monotone-blend fallback when spiral winds past first inflection. Degree-1 polyline caveat; zero-length degenerate guard; negative-alpha treated as positive. LLM tool `nurbs_fresnel_parameterize_curve` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 25 hermetic tests. HONEST: sampling-based, not closed-form; Fresnel monotone blend active for long curves; curvature residual is approximate. Refs: Walton & Meek (2009) ┬з┬з2тАУ3; Bertolazzi & Frego (2015) ┬з3 тАФ `kerf-cad-core/geom/fresnel_parameterize.py`.

**NURBS-CURVE-INFLECTION** тЬЕ тАФ v2 API: `find_curve_inflections(curve, num_samples=200, tol=1e-6)` returns `CurveInflectionReport(inflection_points, num_inflections, max_curvature, min_curvature, is_fair_class_a, warnings, honest_caveat)`; each inflection is an `InflectionPoint(parameter_u, xy_mm, curvature_left, curvature_right, sign_change)`. Signed curvature ╬║(u) = (x'┬╖y'' тИТ y'┬╖x'') / (x'┬▓ + y'┬▓)^1.5 (Piegl-Tiller ┬з5.3; Farin ┬з10.6). Algorithm: sample ╬║(u) at `num_samples` uniform u-values via NURBS 1st/2nd derivatives тЖТ adjacent sign-change detection (|╬║| < tol treated as zero) тЖТ 5-iteration bisection per bracket тЖТ `is_fair_class_a = True` iff тЙд 1 inflection AND no abrupt ╬║-jump (>5├Ч mean, Farin ┬з10.6; Sapidis ┬з3). Legacy v1 API (`find_curve_inflections_v1` тЖТ `InflectionResult`) retained for backward compat. LLM tool `nurbs_find_curve_inflections` updated to return v2 payload. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 38 hermetic tests (20 legacy + 18 new; oracles: S-curve тЖТ 1 inflection + fair, double-S sine тЖТ тЙе2 + not fair, circle тЖТ 0 + fair + ╬║тЙИ1/R, straight line тЖТ 0 + fair + warns). HONEST: **2D only** тАФ 3D space-curve inflections (requiring torsion) not supported; sampling-based, does NOT solve ╬║=0 analytically; near-zero-curvature regions may produce false positives or miss gentle crossings. Refs: Piegl-Tiller ┬з5.3/┬з9.2; Farin ┬з10.6; do Carmo ┬з1.5; Sapidis ┬з3 тАФ `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_inflection.py`.

**NURBS-CURVE-EVOLUTE** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_curve_evolute(curve, num_samples=200, min_curvature=1e-6)` returns `EvoluteResult(evolute_points, t_params, num_samples, num_cusps_detected, cusp_t_params, honest_caveat)`; computes the locus of centres of osculating circles E(t) = C(t) + n╠В(t)/╬║(t) where n╠В is the left-hand unit normal and ╬║ is the signed curvature. Algorithm: sample t тИИ [t_min, t_max] at `num_samples` uniform points; evaluate ╬║(t) via standard plane-curve formula ╬║ = (x'y'' тИТ y'x'')/(x'┬▓+y'┬▓)^(3/2) using NURBS analytical derivatives; skip samples where |╬║| < min_curvature (evolute diverges); detect cusps (vertices of C) as local extrema of |╬║| via windowed comparison with amplitude guard (suppresses floating-point chatter on constant-╬║ curves). Circle oracle: all evolute points within 1.6e-15 of center. Parabola y=x┬▓/2: apex evolute = (0,1) exactly. Ellipse a=2,b=1: 4 cusps (stretched-astroid evolute). Straight line: evolute empty. LLM tool `nurbs_compute_curve_evolute` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 20 hermetic tests. HONEST: **2D curves only** тАФ 3D Frenet-Serret evolutes (requiring torsion) are not yet supported; cusp detection is windowed/amplitude-gated and depends on sample density; may miss cusps for highly undersampled curves. Applications: cycloidal-gear design, cam-profile cusp analysis, CNC offset self-intersection prediction. Refs: do Carmo ┬з1.6; Mortenson ┬з4.2 тАФ `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_evolute.py`.

**NURBS-SURFACE-CROSS-SECTION** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_surface_cross_section(surface, plane_point, plane_normal, nu=50, nv=50)` returns `SurfaceCrossSectionResult(intersection_points_3d, num_intersections, num_components, is_closed_loop, honest_caveat)`; computes the planar cross-section curve C(t) of a NurbsSurface S(u,v) intersected with a plane P (point + normal). Algorithm (Sederberg CAGD ┬з7.3; Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬з5): (1) sample S(u,v) on a (nu ├Ч nv) uniform grid over the knot domain; (2) compute signed distance d(u,v) = (S тИТ P) ┬╖ n╠В for each sample; (3) walk all u-direction and v-direction grid edges, detect sign changes (d_A * d_B < 0); (4) refine each crossing via 5 bisection iterations in (u,v) parameter space (positional error тЙИ cell_size/32); (5) chain intersection points into polyline components via greedy nearest-neighbour walk; (6) detect closed loops (first тЙИ last point within 3├Ч mean spacing). Oracles: sphere R=2 тИй XY plane (mean radius within 20%), cylinder тИй XZ plane (2 components, yтЙИ0), flat patch тИй parallel plane (empty), torus тИй z=0 (inner/outer rings), non-unit normal idempotent, zero normal safe. LLM tool `nurbs_compute_surface_cross_section` registered via gated import. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 22 hermetic tests green. HONEST: **sample-based** тАФ sub-cell features (thin necks, tangential near-grazing crossings) may be missed at low nu/nv; 5-iteration bisection (not sub-pixel for coarse grids); component ordering greedy nearest-neighbour (may mis-order interleaved loops); closed-loop detection threshold-based. Refs: Sederberg CAGD ┬з7.3; Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬з5 тАФ `kerf-cad-core/geom/surface_cross_section.py`.

**NURBS uniform arc-length resample** тЬЕ тАФ `resample_uniform_arc_length(curve, samples=100)` returns `ResampleResult(points, parameters, arc_lengths, total_length, fitted_curve, degenerate)`; arc-length inversion via bisection on adaptive 5-pt Gauss-Legendre integral (Piegl-Tiller ┬з9.4 + Patrikalakis-Maekawa ┬з3.5); `fit=True` returns interpolated NurbsCurve; degenerate flag for zero-length curves; LLM tool `nurbs_curve_resample_uniform`; 12 analytic-oracle tests (circle 2╧А/100 ┬▒ 0.001, parabola arc-uniform < param-uniform variance, line sqrt(2)/10 ┬▒ 1e-6, degenerate flag). Honest: GL quadrature ~1e-9 accurate; highly-oscillatory curves may need larger `max_depth`.
**Mold MFR injection-speed check** тЬЕ тАФ `mold_check_melt_flow_ratio` LLM tool: given a polymer's Melt Flow Rate (ASTM D1238 g/10 min), wall thickness, and gate type, returns the recommended injection-speed envelope to avoid jetting, sink marks, and gate freeze-off. Four MFR bands (low < 5, medium 5тАУ25, high 25тАУ100, super-high > 100 g/10 min); wall-thickness and gate-type correction factors applied; qualitative risk flags for gate freeze, jetting, and sink marks. References: Beaumont 2007 ┬з4 + Menges 2001 ┬з6.2 + ASTM D1238. **Honest caveat**: heuristic only тАФ MFR is a single-point viscosity proxy; real injection-speed tuning requires full shear-thinning viscosity curve and on-tool DOE with cavity-pressure measurement тАФ `kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/melt_flow_ratio_check.py`.

**MOLD-SPRUE-BUSHING-MATCH** тЬЕ тАФ `check_sprue_bushing_match(SprueBushingSpec, MachineNozzleSpec) -> SprueMatchReport` in `kerf_mold.sprue_bushing_match`. Compliance rules: sprue_R = nozzle_r + 0.5тАУ1.0 mm; sprue_O = nozzle_O + 0.5тАУ1.0 mm; taper 1.5тАУ3.0┬░/side. Dataclasses: `SprueBushingSpec` (nozzle_radius_R_mm, sprue_orifice_diameter_O_mm, total_length_mm, taper_per_side_deg); `MachineNozzleSpec` (nozzle_tip_radius_mm, nozzle_tip_orifice_diameter_mm); `SprueMatchReport` (R_mismatch_mm, R_compliant, O_mismatch_mm, O_compliant, taper_compliant, recommendation, honest_caveat).
