**MOLD-COOLING-TURBULENT-RE-CHECK** тЬЕ тАФ `check_turbulent_re(CoolingFlowSpec) -> TurbulentReCheckReport` in `kerf_mold.cooling_turbulent_re_check`. Verifies cooling-channel Reynolds number Re = ╧Б┬╖v┬╖D/╬╝ against the fully-turbulent threshold (Re тЙе 10 000) required for Dittus-Boelter correlation validity (Incropera & DeWitt eq. 8.60: Nu=0.023┬╖Re^0.8┬╖Pr^n). Flow-regime classification (White "Fluid Mechanics" ┬з8.1): Re<2300 тЖТ "laminar" (AVOID тАФ thermally stratified, very poor cooling), 2300тЙдRe<4000 тЖТ "transitional" (unpredictable; avoid), 4000тЙдRe<10000 тЖТ "turbulent" (Dittus-Boelter valid but h sub-optimal), ReтЙе10000 тЖТ "fully_turbulent" (target for mold cooling, Beaumont 2007 ┬з11). Also computes minimum recommended flow rate [L/min] to reach Re=10000 for the given channel geometry and coolant. Dataclasses: `CoolingFlowSpec` (channel_diameter_mm, flow_rate_L_per_min, coolant_density_kg_m3=1000, coolant_viscosity_cP=1.0); `TurbulentReCheckReport` (reynolds_number, flow_regime, velocity_m_per_s, recommended_min_flow_rate_L_per_min, dittus_boelter_applicable, honest_caveat). Unit conversions: mmтЖТm, L/minтЖТm┬│/s├╖60000, cPтЖТPa┬╖s. LLM tool `mold_check_turbulent_re` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 24 tests green. **HONEST SCOPE: Re classification ONLY** тАФ does NOT compute Nusselt number / convective HTC (requires Prandtl number input), polymer-side boundary layer, mold-steel wall thermal resistance, or part-steel contact resistance; does NOT model wall heat flux or non-uniform temperature distribution along the channel; single-phase, isothermal, incompressible, Newtonian fluid only (no two-phase/supercritical COтВВ cooling); viscosity spatially uniform (re-run with exit viscosity for ╬ФT > 10 ┬░C); circular cross-section assumed (non-circular channels: supply hydraulic diameter D_h=4A/P) тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cooling_turbulent_re_check.py`. Refs: Beaumont 2007 ┬з11 (cooling-system Re requirement); White "Fluid Mechanics" 8th ed. ┬з8.1 (Re thresholds); Incropera & DeWitt "Heat and Mass Transfer" 7th ed. ┬з8.5 eq. 8.60 (Dittus-Boelter ReтЙе10000).

**MOLD-CORE-PIN-COOLING** тЬЕ тАФ `design_core_pin_cooling(CorePinSpec) -> CorePinCoolingReport` in `kerf_mold.core_pin_cooling`. Interior baffle/bubbler cooling design for slender injection-mold core pins (tall rib inserts). Re = 4┬╖Q┬╖╧Б/(╧А┬╖D_h┬╖╬╝) (volumetric form); Nusselt number Nu = 0.023┬╖Re^0.8┬╖Pr^0.4 (Dittus-Boelter, Incropera eq. 8.60); HTC h = Nu┬╖k_f/D_h; bubbler mode applies a 2├Ч HTC multiplier relative to baffle per Menges 2001 ┬з7.5 and Beaumont 2007 ┬з11.4 (fountain-effect tip cooling + annular return turbulence). Core-tip temperature from 1-D lumped steady-state resistance network: R_poly = 1/(h_p┬╖A_surface) (h_p = 2000 W/m┬▓K, Menges ┬з7.1 midpoint); R_steel = L_half/(k_steel┬╖A_cross) (k_steel = 15 W/m┬╖K P20/H13); R_cool = 1/(h┬╖A_bore). Cycle-time estimate by Menges 2001 ┬з7.3.3 / Chen-Chiang 1985 first-term Fourier: t_c = (h_wall┬▓/╧А┬▓╬▒)┬╖ln[(8/╧А┬▓)┬╖(T_meltтИТT_cool)/(T_ejectтИТT_cool)]; ╬▒ = 1.0e-7 m┬▓/s (ABS baseline). Oracle (30 mm core, 100 mm tall, baffle, 4 mm ID, 2 L/min water at 20 ┬░C, Pr=7): Re = 10610, Nu = 83.2, HTC = 12445 W/m┬▓K; bubbler HTC = 24890 W/m┬▓K (2.000├Ч ratio); cycle-time = 248 s. `cooling_adequate = True` iff Re тЙе 10 000 AND T_tip тЙд target. `CorePinSpec` dataclass (core_diameter_mm, core_height_mm, baffle_or_bubbler: "baffle"|"bubbler", cooling_type_id_mm, coolant_flow_L_per_min, melt_temp_C, target_core_temp_C, polymer_grade, coolant_temp_C=20, density, viscosity, Pr, k_f); `CorePinCoolingReport` dataclass (reynolds_number, htc_W_per_m2K, estimated_core_tip_temp_C, cooling_adequate, cycle_time_estimate_s, honest_caveat). LLM tool `mold_design_core_pin_cooling` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 33 oracle tests green. **HONEST SCOPE: lumped-capacitance steady-state ONLY** тАФ no transient FEA; uniform melt temperature assumed (no gate-to-far-end gradient); bubbler 2├Ч multiplier is empirical (actual factor depends on tube OD/bore ID ratio, tip clearance, entry turbulence); polymer-side HTC fixed at handbook midpoint 2000 W/m┬▓K (range 1 000тАУ4 000 W/m┬▓K); Dittus-Boelter valid only Re тЙе 10 000 and L/D тЙе 10; cycle-time is 1-D Fourier pin half-diameter only (not full mold cycle); confirm with transient FEA (Moldflow Insight / Moldex3D / SigmaSoft) for production tooling тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/core_pin_cooling.py`. Refs: Menges G., Michaeli W., Mohren P. "How to Make Injection Molds" 3rd ed. Hanser 2001 ┬з7.5 (core-pin cooling) + ┬з7.1 (polymer HTC) + ┬з7.3.3 (cooling-time formula); Beaumont J.P. "Runner and Gating Design Handbook" 2nd ed. Hanser 2007 ┬з11.4 (slender-core cooling; fountain-effect doubling); Incropera & DeWitt "Fundamentals of Heat and Mass Transfer" 7th ed. Wiley 2011 ┬з8.5 eq. 8.60.

**MOLD-EJECTOR-PIN-PUSH** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_ejector_pin_push(EjectorPinPushSpec) -> EjectorPinPushReport` in `kerf_mold.ejector_pin_push`. Computes the Euler critical buckling load for an SPI/ANSI B151.1 ejector pin and verifies it against the required push force. Formula: F_cr = ╧А┬▓┬╖E┬╖I/(K┬╖L)┬▓  (Roark's 9e ┬з15.2); I = ╧А┬╖dтБ┤/64 (solid round section); E = 200 GPa for all tool-steel grades (M2_tool_steel, H13, S7, D2 тАФ all share the same nominal Young's modulus). End-condition coefficient K: 1.0 pinned-pinned (SPI/ANSI B151.1 default for guided pins), 0.5 fixed-fixed, 0.7 fixed-pinned, 2.0 cantilever. Dataclasses: `EjectorPinPushSpec` (pin_diameter_mm, pin_length_L_mm, pin_material: "M2_tool_steel"|"H13"|"S7"|"D2", end_condition_K=1.0, required_push_force_N); `EjectorPinPushReport` (buckling_force_N, dcr=required/F_cr, adequate: bool, recommended_min_diameter_mm, recommended_pin_material, honest_caveat). Recommendation logic: searches SPI standard diameters (1, 1.5, 2, 2.5, 3, 4, 5, 6, 8, 10, 12, 16, 20 mm) for the smallest diameter with F_cr тЙе 1.1 ├Ч required_push_force_N at the same L and K; prefers M2 when DCR > 0.8. Numeric oracle: 8 mm, L=100 mm, K=1: F_cr = ╧А┬│┬╖200000┬╖64/10000 тЙИ 39 688 N; 4 mm pin is 16├Ч weaker than 8 mm (I тИЭ dтБ┤); doubling L reduces F_cr by 4├Ч. LLM tool `mold_compute_ejector_pin_push` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 45 oracle tests green. **HONEST SCOPE: Euler formula only** тАФ non-conservative for short/stout pins (K┬╖L/d < 30); use Johnson parabolic formula F_cr_J = A┬╖╧Г_y┬╖[1 тИТ ╧Г_y┬╖(K┬╖L/r)┬▓/(4┬╖╧А┬▓┬╖E)] in that regime (function flags the warning in honest_caveat); bushing friction (╬╝тЙИ0.05тАУ0.10 lubricated, reduces capacity 3тАУ10 %) and pin eccentricity/TIR beam-column amplification (Roark's 9e ┬з15.3) are NOT modelled; dynamic ejection impact and fatigue over millions of cycles are NOT assessed; confirm by mold-trial load-cell measurement тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/ejector_pin_push.py`. Refs: SPI/ANSI B151.1; Roark R.J. & Young W.C. Formulas for Stress and Strain, 9th ed., ┬з15.2тАУ15.3; ASM Handbook Vol.1 (tool-steel E values).

**MOLD-TUNNEL-GATE-DESIGN** тЬЕ тАФ `design_tunnel_gate(TunnelGateSpec) -> TunnelGateReport` in `kerf_mold.tunnel_gate_design`. Designs a tunnel (submarine) gate given part weight and polymer grade. Diameter: D = 0.5 ├Ч wall_thickness (Beaumont 2007 ┬з7.4); +10 % high-viscosity correction for PC/PA66/PMMA/POM/PEI/PPO; lower bound 0.8 mm (machining floor); upper cap D тЙд 2/3 ├Ч wall_thickness (Menges 2001 ┬з6.6.5). Break-off force: F = ╧Д_shear ├Ч ╧А/4┬╖D┬▓ using Menges 2001 Table 6.3 shear strengths (ABS=30, PC=45, PP=22, PA66=40, POM=38, PMMA=42, PEI=50, PPO=45 MPa). Shear rate: ╬│╠З = 4Q/(╧А┬╖r┬│) (Hagen-Poiseuille, Newtonian); Q = (m_part/╧Б_melt) / 1.0 s; Beaumont ┬з7.4 limit 50 000 sтБ╗┬╣; `shear_within_limit` flag. Gate freeze time: t_f = (D┬▓/╧А┬▓┬╖╬▒)┬╖ln[(8/╧А┬▓)┬╖(T_meltтИТT_mold)/(T_ejectтИТT_mold)] per Chen-Chiang ANTEC 1985 / Menges 2001 ┬з7.3.3. Angle recommendation: 30┬░ for flexible/low-viscosity, 45┬░ for stiff/high-viscosity (Menges ┬з6.6.5). Oracle: ABS, 30 g, wall 2 mm тЖТ D = 1.0 mm; F_break = 23.6 N; freeze time тЙИ 1.42 s. `TunnelGateSpec` (part_weight_g, wall_thickness_at_gate_mm, polymer_grade, melt_temp_C, gate_angle_deg=30.0, gate_length_mm=1.5); `TunnelGateReport` (gate_diameter_mm, gate_break_off_force_N, gate_freeze_time_s, shear_rate_at_gate_per_s, shear_within_limit, recommended_angle_deg, honest_caveat). LLM tool `mold_design_tunnel_gate` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 35 tests green. **HONEST: Beaumont heuristic тАФ diameter is a start-point only; complex multi-cavity timing and fill-pressure balance require Moldflow/Moldex3D full 3-D fill simulation; break-off force sensitive to mold temperature and specific resin grade ductility; shear rate is Newtonian approximation (actual shear-thinning ╬│╠З тЙИ 1.25тАУ1.5├Ч higher); freeze time is 1-D Fourier constant-diffusivity (PP/PA66/POM actual 15тАУ25 % longer due to crystallisation latent heat); confirm by mold trial** тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/tunnel_gate_design.py`. Refs: Beaumont J.P. "Runner and Gating Design Handbook" 2nd ed. Hanser 2007 ┬з7.4; Menges G., Michaeli W., Mohren P. "How to Make Injection Molds" 3rd ed. Hanser 2001 ┬з6.6.5 + Table 6.3 + ┬з7.3.3; Chen-Chiang ANTEC 1985.

**MOLD-SURFACE-FINISH-CHECK** тЬЕ тАФ `check_surface_finish(SurfaceFinishSpec, MoldSpec) -> SurfaceFinishReport` in `kerf_mold.surface_finish_check`. Validates that a molded part's resin + mold-steel + hardness combination can achieve the requested SPI Mold Finish Standard grade (A1тАУD3), and recommends mold steel grade, minimum HRC, and polishing method. SPI grades (2017 standard): A1 Ra тЙд 0.012 ┬╡m (diamond paste #3, S136 тЙе50 HRC), A2 Ra тЙд 0.025 ┬╡m (diamond buff #6, S136 тЙе48 HRC), A3 Ra тЙд 0.050 ┬╡m (diamond buff #15, S136/H13 тЙе44 HRC); B1 Ra тЙд 0.10 ┬╡m (600-grit stone, H13 тЙе38 HRC), B2тАУB3 Ra 0.20тАУ0.40 ┬╡m (stone, P20); C1тАУC3 Ra 0.80тАУ3.20 ┬╡m (emery cloth, P20); D1тАУD3 Ra 3.2тАУ14 ┬╡m (dry blast, P20). Glass-fiber rule (Menges ┬з11.4.2): glass-reinforced resins cannot achieve A-grade on the molded part regardless of mold polish (fiber pull-out + print-through). Resin limits: PA66 тЖТ max A3 (crystalline skin haze); PP тЖТ max B1; POM тЖТ max B2; LDPE тЖТ max C1. Steel limits: S136 тЖТ A1; 420SS тЖТ A2; H13 тЖТ A3; P20 тЖТ B3. Dataclasses: `SurfaceFinishSpec` (required_finish, resin); `MoldSpec` (mold_steel, hardness_HRC, mold_finish_achieved=""); `SurfaceFinishReport` (achievable, recommended_steel, recommended_hardness_HRC_min, recommended_polishing_method, Ra_target_um, Ra_achievable_um, glass_filled_warning, honest_caveat). LLM tool `mold_check_surface_finish` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 27 tests green. **HONEST: catalog-based checker тАФ does NOT model texture chemistry (etching achievability depends on etch bath + resin crystallinity), etcher capability (bath concentration + cycle count not modelled), polishing wear-life (abrasive filler content + shot count not modelled), part-geometry effects (weld lines + deep ribs harder to polish), or process variables (mold temperature, hold pressure, cooling time affect surface replication fidelity)** тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/surface_finish_check.py`. Refs: SPI/PLASTICS Mold Finish Standards 2017; Menges G., Mohren P. "How to Make Injection Molds" 3rd ed. Hanser 2001 ┬з11; Bryce D. M. "Plastic Injection Molding: Mold Design and Construction Fundamentals" SME 1998 Ch. 8.

**MOLD-COLOR-CONCENTRATE-RATIO** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_color_ratio(ColorConcentrateSpec, ShotSpec) -> ColorRatioReport` in `kerf_mold.color_concentrate_ratio`. Gravimetric let-down ratio (LDR) dosing and mixing-quality assessment for color concentrate (masterbatch) in injection moulding. LDR formula (SPI Color Concentrates Handbook 3rd ed. ┬з3): LDR (%) = target_pigment_loading_pct / pigment_loading_in_masterbatch_pct ├Ч 100. Masterbatch per shot [g] = shot_weight_g ├Ч LDR/100; masterbatch per kg natural resin [g/kg] = 1000 ├Ч (LDR/100) / (1 тИТ LDR/100). SPI recommended LDR range: 1тАУ5 %. Mixing index heuristic (Menges Plastics Manufacturing ┬з10.2; Tadmor & Gogos ┬з12.5): mixing_index = 1 тИТ exp(тИТbarrel_residence_s ├Ч screw_L/D / 200); adequate if > 0.80. Streaking-risk classification: low (LDR 1тАУ5 % AND mixing_index > 0.80), moderate (marginal LDR 0.5тАУ1 % or 5тАУ8 %, or mixing_index тЙд 0.80 with LDR in range), high (LDR < 0.5 % тАФ too dilute for shot-to-shot uniformity тАФ or LDR > 8 % тАФ cost-waste territory / mechanical-property dilution risk per Menges ┬з10.4). Dataclasses: `ColorConcentrateSpec` (pigment_loading_in_masterbatch_pct, recommended_let_down_pct, carrier_resin, melting_temp_C); `ShotSpec` (shot_weight_g, target_pigment_loading_pct, barrel_residence_time_s, screw_L_over_D=20.0); `ColorRatioReport` (let_down_ratio_pct, masterbatch_per_shot_g, masterbatch_per_kg_natural, mixing_index_estimate, color_streaking_risk, warnings, honest_caveat). Oracle: 100 g shot, target 1 % pigment, MB at 40 % тЖТ LDR = 2.5 %, MB = 2.5 g/shot, MB per kg natural тЙИ 25.64 g/kg. LLM tool `mold_compute_color_concentrate_ratio` registered in plugin.py; re-exported from `kerf_mold/__init__.py`. 40 tests green. **HONEST: mixing index is a heuristic exponential-decay proxy from L/D and residence time only тАФ does NOT model screw-flight geometry, back-pressure, screw speed, melt-viscosity mismatch between masterbatch carrier and natural resin, pellet size ratio, or colorant particle agglomerate size; LDR is gravimetric only (volumetric accuracy requires density-matched MB and natural resin); streaking-risk classification is a screening guideline тАФ trial colour plaques with L*a*b* colorimetric measurement per ISO 11664-4 are the only reliable acceptance test; carrier resin compatibility must be confirmed against base resin; empirical mixing estimate, NOT a substitute for colour-master trial shots** тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/color_concentrate_ratio.py`. Refs: SPI "Color Concentrates Handbook" 3rd ed. ┬з3, ┬з6, ┬з8, ┬з11; Menges G., Kemper B., Klenk E. "Plastics Manufacturing" ┬з10; Tadmor Z. & Gogos C. "Principles of Polymer Processing" 2nd ed. Wiley 2006, ┬з12.5.

**ARCH-BASE-PLATE-AISC (AISC DG-1 ┬з3.1 + AISC 360-22 ┬зJ8)** тЬЕ тАФ `design_base_plate(ColumnSpec, ConcreteSpec, Fy=345.0) -> BasePlateReport` implements steel column base plate design for concentric axial compressive loads. Concrete bearing strength: Pp = 0.85┬╖f'c┬╖A1┬╖тИЪ(A2/A1) with A2/A1 тЙд 4 (AISC 360-22 ┬зJ8 Eq J8-2); ╧Ж_c = 0.65; required A1 = P_u/(╧Ж_c┬╖0.85┬╖f'c┬╖тИЪ(A2/A1)). Plate dimensions rounded up to nearest 5 mm; must cover column footprint (0.95┬╖d ├Ч 0.80┬╖bf per DG-1 ┬з3.1.1). Cantilever arms: m=(NтИТ0.95┬╖d)/2 (Eq 3.1-1); n=(BтИТ0.80┬╖bf)/2 (Eq 3.1-2); n'=тИЪ(d┬╖bf)/4; X=[4┬╖d┬╖bf/(d+bf)┬▓]┬╖[P_u/(╧Ж_c┬╖Pp)] (Eq 3.1-8); ╬╗=min(1, 2┬╖тИЪX/(1+тИЪ(1тИТX))); l=max(m,n,╬╗┬╖n'). Plate thickness via Murray-Stockwell (DG-1 Eq 3.1-5): t=l┬╖тИЪ(2┬╖P_u/(0.9┬╖Fy┬╖B┬╖N)), rounded up to 1 mm. Oracle: W14x90, P=1000 kN, f'c=30 MPa, ped 600├Ч600 mm тЖТ A1_reqтЙИ30166 mm┬▓; plate 295├Ч340 mm (column footprint governs, N_min=338 mm, B_min=295 mm); t=15 mm; DCR=0.318 (adequate). `arch_design_base_plate` LLM tool registered in plugin (gated import). Re-exported from arch/__init__.py. 24 hermetic oracle tests pass тАФ `packages/kerf-cad-core/src/kerf_cad_core/arch/base_plate_aisc.py`. *SCOPE: concentric axial compressive load ONLY (DG-1 ┬з3.1). NOT covered: moment transfer (DG-1 ┬з3.2), anchor rod design (DG-1 ┬з3.3тАУ3.4), shear lug (DG-1 ┬з3.5), biaxial bending, tensile uplift. A2 taken as pedestal plan area; irregular pedestals must supply equivalent rectangular A2. Grout strength тЙе f'c assumed.*

**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ **MOLD-EJECTOR-STROKE-VERIFY** (Beaumont 2007 ┬з9 + Menges 2001 ┬з7.4): `verify_ejector_stroke()` тАФ (1) stroke adequacy: required_stroke (part_depth + safety_margin) тЙд machine_stroke; (2) force capacity: pin_count ├Ч max_force тЙе ejection_force (Menges ┬з7.4); (3) pin deflection: ╬┤=F┬╖L┬│/(3┬╖E┬╖I) тЙд 0.05mm allowable (Euler-Bernoulli cantilever, Beaumont ┬з9.3, I=╧А┬╖dтБ┤/64, E=200 GPa steel); (4) knockout bar contact: plate_thickness тЙе bar_diameter (Beaumont ┬з9.5); `EjectorStrokeReport` dataclass (stroke_adequate, force_per_pin, max_deflection_mm, violations); LLM tool `mold_verify_ejector_stroke` registered; 33 oracle tests; static load only (honest-flagged: no dynamic ejection force, shrinkage grip, thermal expansion, or pin fatigue) тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/ejector_stroke_verify.py` тЬЕ.

**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ **MOLD-COOLING-TIME-CHEN-CHIANG** (Chen-Chiang 1985 + Menges 2001 ┬з7.3.3 + Beaumont 2007 ┬з10.4): `compute_cooling_time_chen_chiang()` тАФ 1-D Fourier first-term cooling-time formula: t_c = (h┬▓/╧А┬▓╬▒)┬╖ln[(8/╧А┬▓)┬╖(T_mтИТT_w)/(T_eтИТT_w)]; `MaterialThermalProps` dataclass (name, thermal_diffusivity_m2_per_s, T_melt_C, T_ejection_C); `CoolingTimeReport` dataclass (wall_thickness_mm, cooling_time_s, dominant_factor, material_used, honest_caveat); MATERIAL_THERMAL_DB (Menges 2001 Table 7.3): ABS ╬▒=1.00e-7, PC ╬▒=1.50e-7, PP ╬▒=0.95e-7, PA66 ╬▒=1.40e-7, POM ╬▒=0.95e-7, PMMA ╬▒=1.13e-7 m┬▓/s; dominant-factor diagnosis (thickness_squared|diffusivity|temp_window) via log-sensitivity; LLM tool `mold_compute_cooling_time_chen_chiang` registered; 24 oracle tests; honest-flagged: 1-D Fourier first-term approximation only тАФ ignores cooling-channel layout and conformal-cooling effects; does NOT model crystallisation latent heat (semi-crystalline PP/PA66/POM times 15тАУ30% longer), thermal contact resistance, or hot-spot effects from varying wall thickness; use Moldflow/Moldex3D/SigmaSoft for a full cooling-circuit simulation тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cooling_time_chen_chiang.py` тЬЕ.
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ **MOLD-RUNNER-BALANCE-CHECK** (Beaumont 2007 ┬з6.6 + Menges 2001 ┬з6.6.4): `check_runner_balance()` тАФ Hagen-Poiseuille hydraulic resistance path check for multi-cavity runner networks; R_norm = L/rтБ┤ per segment (╬╝ cancels in ratios); path resistance summed sprueтЖТgate via parent-pointer walk; max_imbalance_pct = 100├Ч(R_maxтИТR_min)/R_mean; balanced=True iff max_imbalance_pct < 5 % (Beaumont 2007 ┬з6.6 criterion); `RunnerSegment` dataclass (id, length_mm, diameter_mm, parent_id); `RunnerBalanceReport` dataclass (cavity_paths[{cavity_id, total_length_mm, total_resistance, fill_ratio}], max_imbalance_pct, balanced, honest_caveat); LLM tool `mold_check_runner_balance` registered; 42 oracle tests; honest-flagged: geometric resistance only тАФ does NOT model temperature-dependent or shear-thinning viscosity, shear-heating asymmetry in graduated-diameter (artificially balanced) runners (Beaumont RPI runner), or transient filling inertia; use Moldflow/Moldex3D/SigmaSoft for full rheological fill simulation тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/runner_balance_check.py` тЬЕ.
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ mold draft-angle validation per face: arcsin(|n╠В┬╖pull╠В|) draft angle; SPI finish grades A1тАУD3 minimum lookup (Menges 2001 ┬з3.4 + Beaumont 2007 ┬з4); region-aware minimums (outer 0.5┬░, inner 1.0┬░, rib 1.0┬░, boss 0.5┬░); top/bottom face pass-through; degenerate-normal flagging; LLM tool `mold_validate_draft`; 38 oracle tests; v1 honest-flag: undercut detection out of scope тЬЕ.
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ adaptive/trochoidal CAM HSM + rest machining; moldflow Hele-Shaw front tracking + weld-line + air-trap; casting Chvorinov + riser sizing + gating; NFP true-shape polygon nesting (57.6 % L-shape utilisation); **NFP + GA nesting optimizer** (Burke 2006 + Kovacs 2002): `optimize_nest()` тАФ bottom-left-fill + GA sequence/rotation search, 50 generations, 82.4 % L-shape utilisation (91├Ч35 sheet, seed=42), `manufacturing_optimize_nest` LLM tool registered, 23 tests.
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ adaptive/trochoidal CAM HSM + rest machining; moldflow Hele-Shaw front tracking + weld-line + air-trap; casting Chvorinov + riser sizing + gating; NFP true-shape polygon nesting (57.6 % L-shape utilisation). **MANUFACTURING-TOOLING-CATALOG-MATCH** тЬЕ тАФ `match_tooling(operation, material, dimension_mm) тЖТ ToolingMatchResult`; embedded 50-tool catalog (Sandvik, Iscar, Kennametal, OSG, Tungaloy); end mills/drills/taps/reamers/inserts; speeds+feeds per workpiece material (SFM + IPT); `manufacturing_match_tooling` LLM tool; 70 hermetic tests. Honest flag: ~50-tool sample catalog; verify against CoroPlus/Iscar ITA for production. Refs: Sandvik Cutting Data Rec. 2024; Drozda-Wick ┬з3 (SME 4th ed.).
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ adaptive/trochoidal CAM HSM + rest machining; moldflow Hele-Shaw front tracking + weld-line + air-trap; casting Chvorinov + riser sizing + gating; NFP true-shape polygon nesting (57.6 % L-shape utilisation); **cutting-speed database** (20 workpiece materials ├Ч 4 tool materials ├Ч 4 ops = 320 entries, Machinery's Handbook 31e ┬з1100 + Sandvik CoroKey; `manufacturing_query_cutting_speed` LLM tool).
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ adaptive/trochoidal CAM HSM + rest machining; G83 peck-drilling canned cycle (NIST RS-274/NGC ┬з3.8.4 + MH 31e ┬з1132, time estimate excludes acceleration ramps); G84/G74 rigid tapping canned cycle (NIST RS-274/NGC ┬з3.8.4 + MH 31e ┬з1934 feed coupling F=pitch├Чrpm; M29 Fanuc rigid-tap engage; right-hand G84 + left-hand G74; honest caveat: floating tap holders not modelled); moldflow Hele-Shaw front tracking + weld-line + air-trap; casting Chvorinov + riser sizing + gating; NFP true-shape polygon nesting (57.6 % L-shape utilisation).
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ adaptive/trochoidal CAM HSM + rest machining; moldflow Hele-Shaw front tracking + weld-line + air-trap; casting Chvorinov + riser sizing + gating; NFP true-shape polygon nesting (57.6 % L-shape utilisation); injection-mold gate-vestige estimation + cosmetic-class compliance (Beaumont 2007 ┬з7.6 Table 7.4; Menges 2001 ┬з6.6 тАФ edge/tunnel/submarine/hot_tip/pin_point/fan/film gates, A1тАУC cosmetic classes; empirical estimates only тАФ actual vestige depends on degating tool sharpness, melt temp, and resin grade ductility).
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ **MOLD-DRAFT-DEMOLD-FORCE** (Beaumont 2007 ┬з9.3 + Menges 2001 ┬з7.4 + Table 7.6): `compute_demold_force()` тАФ cavity-ejection force per F = ╬╝┬╖╧Г_h┬╖A┬╖cos╬▒/(cos╬▒ + ╬╝┬╖sin╬▒); shrinkage stress ╧Г_h from Menges Table 7.6 (ABS=4.0, PC=3.0, PP=5.0, PA66=3.5, POM=4.5 MPa); friction ╬╝ from SPI finish class (SPI_A1=0.15 polished тАж SPI_D1=0.40 textured); `MoldedPartSpec` dataclass (polymer_grade, contact_area_cm2, draft_angle_deg, mold_steel_finish_class); `DemoldForceReport` dataclass (demold_force_N, contact_pressure_MPa, ejector_pin_count_required, friction_coeff_used, polymer_shrinkage_stress_MPa, honest_caveat); ejector pin count = ceil(F / single_pin_capacity_N); LLM tool `mold_compute_demold_force` registered; 28 oracle tests; honest-flagged: empirical formula only тАФ ignores chemical adhesion (resin stick, relevant for PC/POM on polished steel), undercut/side-action geometry, dynamic ejection force, and pin fatigue; confirm by mold-trial load-cell measurement тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/demold_force_check.py` тЬЕ.
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ **MOLD-VENT-DEPTH-CHECK** (Beaumont 2007 ┬з8.3 Table 8.2 + Menges 2001 ┬з6.4 Table 6.7): `check_vent_depth()` тАФ verify that a mold parting-line vent depth (air-escape gap) is within the polymer-specific recommended range; too shallow тЖТ trapped air тЖТ short shot / burn marks (diesel effect); too deep тЖТ flash; polymer database (mm): ABS 0.025тАУ0.038, PC 0.013тАУ0.025, PP 0.025тАУ0.050, PA66 0.013тАУ0.025, POM 0.013тАУ0.025, PMMA 0.025тАУ0.038, PE 0.038тАУ0.075; `VentSpec` dataclass (polymer_grade, proposed_depth_mm, land_length_mm=1.5, vent_width_mm=6.0); `VentDepthReport` dataclass (recommended_depth_min_mm, recommended_depth_max_mm, compliant, depth_class, polymer_notes, honest_caveat); depth_class: "too_shallow"|"correct"|"too_deep"|"flash_risk" (>25% above max); unknown polymers receive fallback range [0.013тАУ0.038 mm] with caveat; LLM tool `mold_check_vent_depth` registered; 35 oracle tests; honest-flagged: empirical handbook ranges only тАФ actual safe vent depth depends on resin batch viscosity, melt temperature, injection speed, mold surface finish, land length, and part geometry; filled/FR/rubber-toughened grades may flash within the correct band for base resin; confirm by mold trial + visual flash inspection тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/vent_depth_check.py` тЬЕ.
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ **MOLD-VENT-SLOT-LAYOUT** (Beaumont 2007 ┬з8.5 Vent Slot Count and Width + Menges 2001 ┬з6.4): `generate_vent_slot_layout()` тАФ propose vent slot count, width (6 mm standard), and spacing for a parting-line perimeter given cavity volume, polymer grade, and injection speed; Beaumont 0.5 %-projected-area rule: total_vent_area тЙе 0.005 ├Ч cavity_volume_mm┬│/wall_thickness; speed scaling: vent_area_factor = max(1.0, injection_speed / 50 cm┬│/s); per-slot area = 6 mm width ├Ч depth_mid ├Ч 6 mm land length (polymer-specific depth from Beaumont Table 8.2); minimum 4 slots (one per quadrant, Beaumont ┬з8.5; Menges ┬з6.4); maximum slots = floor(perimeter / (6 + 10 mm steel bridge)); spacing = perimeter / n_slots; `MoldVolumeSpec` dataclass (cavity_volume_cm3, parting_line_perimeter_mm, polymer_grade, injection_speed_cm3_s); `VentSlotLayoutReport` dataclass (num_vent_slots, vent_slot_width_mm, vent_slot_spacing_mm, total_vent_width_mm, air_displacement_rate_cm3_s, adequate, honest_caveat); LLM tool `mold_generate_vent_slot_layout` registered; 47 oracle tests; honest-flagged: heuristic 0.5 %-area rule from production experience тАФ NOT a first-principles fluid-dynamic calculation; wall thickness assumed 3 mm for area estimation; uniform spacing only (use mold_optimize_vent_placement for last-to-fill location optimisation); vent depth handled separately by mold_check_vent_depth; confirm by fill simulation (Moldflow / Moldex3D / SigmaSoft) + mold-trial visual inspection тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/vent_slot_layout.py` тЬЕ.
**Manufacturing depth** тЬЕ тАФ **MOLD-RUNNER-COLD-SLUG** (Beaumont 2007 ┬з6.7 Cold Slug Wells + Menges 2001 ┬з6.5): `check_cold_slug_design()` тАФ verify cold-slug well dimensions at runner junctions in a multi-cavity mold to trap the cold leading-edge polymer melt before it reaches the gate, preventing flow lines and weak weld lines; Beaumont rule: slug well diameter = 1.5 ├Ч runner diameter, depth = 2.0 ├Ч runner diameter, ┬▒20 % tolerance band (1.2├ЧтАУ1.8├Ч diameter, 1.6├ЧтАУ2.4├Ч depth); `RunnerJunctionSpec` dataclass (junction_id, runner_diameter_mm, slug_well_diameter_mm, slug_well_depth_mm, polymer_grade); `ColdSlugReport` dataclass (junction_results list, total_junctions, compliant_count, honest_caveat); per-junction result: diameter_compliant, depth_compliant, slug_well_compliant, recommended_diameter_mm, recommended_depth_mm, tolerance bounds, reason; LLM tool `mold_check_cold_slug_design` registered; 32 oracle tests; honest-flagged: geometric rule-of-thumb only тАФ actual cold-slug capture depends on melt temperature, injection speed, and resin freeze-off time; fast-crystallising resins (POM, PA66, LCP) and filled grades may require larger wells; confirm by mold trial + gate-area visual inspection; use Moldflow / Moldex3D / SigmaSoft for full melt-front thermal and weld-line simulation тАФ `packages/kerf-mold/src/kerf_mold/cold_slug_check.py` тЬЕ.
