### Long-tail verticals

Everything committed, lowest priority. Ordered roughly by near-term readiness.

**Mechanical / product:** cams generators ┬╖ woodworking / furniture / joinery + cutlist ┬╖ power one-line / switchgear ┬╖ lighting / photometric ┬╖ interior / space-planning / FF&E *(IFC 4 export (ISO 16739-1:2018) тЬЕ тАФ subset export, NOT buildingSMART certified; `kerf-interior/ifc_export.py`)* ┬╖ kitchen / bath / cabinetry / millwork ┬╖ landscape ┬╖ scaffolding / formwork.

| Woodworking | Capability | Status |
|---|---|---|
| Joinery geometry validator (Hammer-Krenov) | Validate dovetail (7┬░тАУ14┬░ pin angle, тЙе1/3 board pin width, тЙе2 pins), mortise-and-tenon (1/3-rule, cheek check, tenon length), box joint (тЙе3 fingers, equal widths, depth==thickness), finger joint (angle 15┬▒3┬░); strength estimate via FPL Wood Handbook shear values ├Ч joint efficiency for oak/pine/cherry/maple/walnut in kN; `woodworking_validate_joinery` + `woodworking_joinery_strength` LLM tools | тЬЕ shipped тАФ `kerf-woodworking/joinery_validate.py` |
**Mechanical / product:** cams generators ┬╖ woodworking / furniture / joinery + cutlist ┬╖ power one-line / switchgear ┬╖ lighting / photometric ┬╖ interior / space-planning / FF&E ┬╖ kitchen / bath / cabinetry / millwork ┬╖ landscape (plant catalog with USDA + Dirr references, 101 species тЬЕ) ┬╖ scaffolding / formwork.

**Vehicles:** composites ply/layup authoring (draping / fiber-steering / Fibersim class) ┬╖ hull fairing (NURBS-reachable) ┬╖ 3D harness routing.

**Civil / infrastructure (distinct engines):** plan-and-profile sheet engine ┬╖ IFC-4.3-infra I/O ┬╖ bridge/tunnel ┬╖ mining ┬╖ marine/dredging ┬╖ rail signaling. *(CRS engine, horizontal/vertical alignment, corridor, earthworks, geotechnical, LandXML 1.2 I/O, pressurized water-distribution networks (Todini GGA + Hazen-Williams/Darcy-Weisbach), gravity sewer (Manning), storm rational method + HDS-5 culverts already shipped; TINView / PipeNetworkView / GradingPlanView / LandscapeView UIs тЬЕ 2026-05-29.)*

**Body-worn / medical / craft:** watchmaking / horology ┬╖ eyewear / frames ┬╖ footwear / last design ┬╖ dental CAD (crowns/aligners) ┬╖ orthopedic / prosthetics ┬╖ hearing aids.

**Soft goods (distinct 2D/developable engine):** apparel / pattern-making + drape ┬╖ technical textiles / sails / membrane / tensile ┬╖ upholstery / leather. *(ARAP/LSCM pattern flattening for non-developable surfaces (Bo-Wang 2007 / L├йvy 2002) тЬЕ тАФ `kerf-apparel/pattern_flatten.py`, `apparel_flatten_pattern` LLM tool wired.)*
**Soft goods (distinct 2D/developable engine):** apparel / pattern-making + drape ┬╖ technical textiles / sails / membrane / tensile ┬╖ upholstery / leather. *(ASTM D5219 + ISO 8559 grading rules тЬЕ тАФ `GradingRule`, `build_grading_table`, `apply_grading`, `grade_check_iso_8559` shipped; `apparel_apply_grading` + `apparel_grade_check` LLM tools registered тАФ `packages/kerf-apparel/src/kerf_apparel/grading.py`.)*

**Scientific / niche:** microfluidics / MEMS ┬╖ signage / large-format.

**Silicon next:** verification depth + post-silicon (cocotb testbench harness, power analysis, STA, clock-tree synthesis, formal equivalence, Tiny Tapeout / Efabless harnesses). T-249..T-258.

**Firmware next:** RTOS primitives, OTA, RTOS-aware debugger, power profiling, pin-map cross-check vs PCB, USB-class drivers. T-259..T-265. **T-274 тЬЕ** тАФ Build / Flash / Monitor UI wired: `FirmwareProjectPanel`, `BuildOutput`, `SerialMonitor` in `src/components/firmware/`; `firmware_project` kind renders in Editor; PlatformIO + Arduino IDE compare rows added.

**Aerospace next:** XFOIL-class viscous solver, aircraft conceptual sizing (Raymer/Roskam), stability derivatives, aero-acoustics (FW-H), heat-shield/ablation, aerospace fasteners. T-266..T-272.

**Platform (demand-gated post-launch):** fully-local / offline / no-account desktop app тАФ committed but not a launch pillar. Portability + two-way sync + easy self-host is the launch answer.

### Strategic AI-native capabilities

These are roadmap-level moats that span every sector simultaneously and compound leverage instead of adding it linearly.

| Capability | Status |
|---|---|
| **Generative / topology / multi-objective optimization** тАФ manufacturing-constrained, multi-load-case, lattice-infill. Basic single-objective SIMP shipped; production-grade unbuilt. | ЁЯЪз in flight |
| **Simulation pillar** тАФ nonlinear FEA, explicit dynamics / crash, fatigue & durability, CFD (full turbulence), low/high-frequency EM, acoustics FEM, coupled multiphysics. Linear-static + modal + steady thermal + linear eigenvalue buckling + harmonic (mode-superposition) frequency response + random-vibration PSD (modal + Miles) + CFD 2-D laminar shipped. **FEA UI panels** тЬЕ тАФ 5 solve panels (LinearStaticPanel, ModalPanel, BucklingPanel, FatiguePanel, VibrationPanel) wired in right-drawer FEA tab тАФ `src/components/fea/`. | ЁЯЪз in flight |
| **Automatic Feature Recognition (AFR)** тАФ turns any imported "dumb" STEP into an editable parametric feature tree; critical for the LLM to edit any model, not just ones authored in Kerf. | тЬЕ complete тАФ AAG-based classifier (through-hole, blind-hole, counterbore, countersink, pocket, slot, boss, fillet, chamfer, rib, step) + topology ordering into a replay-able parametric DAG (`afr_to_dag`) + `.feature` log emitter + `afr_to_parametric` LLM tool registered тАФ `kerf-cad-core/afr/recognize.py`, `afr/dag.py`, `geom/feature_recognition.py` |
| **Knowledge-based engineering / code-compliance** тАФ AISC/ACI/Eurocode/ASME/ISO rules driven directly by the model. Shipped: AISC 360-22 + ACI 318-19 + EC2/3/5/8 + NDS 2018 + ASCE 7-22 + ISO 6336 + IAPWS-IF97 + IEEE 1584 + IEC 60255. General KBE configurator layer unbuilt. | ЁЯЪз in flight |

| **Automatic Feature Recognition (AFR)** тАФ turns any imported "dumb" STEP into an editable parametric feature tree; critical for the LLM to edit any model, not just ones authored in Kerf. | ЁЯЪз in flight тАФ AAG-based classifier (through-hole, blind-hole, counterbore, countersink, pocket, slot, boss, fillet, chamfer, rib, step) shipped with tests; full topology ordering into a replay-able parametric tree is the remaining step тАФ `kerf-cad-core/afr/recognize.py`, `geom/feature_recognition.py` |

FEA-grade topology repair for severely degenerate STEP not yet covered. | ЁЯЪз in flight |
| **Reverse-engineering pipeline** тАФ point cloud тЖТ segmentation тЖТ feature fit тЖТ parametric solid. | ЁЯЪз in flight тАФ full pipeline shipped: PLY/PCD I/O, outlier removal, sequential-RANSAC segmentation for plane/sphere/cylinder/cone/torus, feature-map classification, ICP mesh registration (dental) тАФ `kerf-cad-core/reverse_engineering/pipeline.py`, `kerf-dental/registration.py`. Topology ordering + freeform NURBS fit deferred (depends on NURBS kernel). |
| **Mechanism synthesis & motion** тАФ linkage / cam / gear-train *synthesis*. | ЁЯЪз in flight тАФ four-bar (Burmester), cam-profile, and gear-train synthesis shipped with reference-oracle tests тАФ `kerf-mates/synthesis/{fourbar,cam,gear_train}.py`. Multi-body dynamic simulation (kerf-motion integrator) also shipped. Assembly motion UI (AssemblyMotionPanel) wired with joint-list editor, Run button, and timeline scrubber. Table-driver inverse-dynamics тЬЕ тАФ position-vs-time table now drives joints via ╧Д=I┬╖╬▒+c┬╖╧Й (`kerf-motion/forces.py:table_driver_torque`). |

### Multi-month epics

- **GK-P foundational kernel** тАФ general solid boolean for NURBS-faced bodies; Stam limit-tangents тЬЕ + G1 at extraordinary SubD points; fractional creases; MatchSrf G3; analytic surface derivatives.

- **GK-P Bezier extraction** тЬЕ тАФ B-spline тЖТ multi-Bezier patch decomposition (Piegl & Tiller ┬з5.6); foundational for FEA tet-mesh handoff, GPU-friendly rendering, IGES export. (`bezier_extract.py`, LLM tool `bezier_extract` registered.)
- **NURBS-CONVERT-TO-IGES-144** тЬЕ тАФ full IGES 5.3 ┬з4.27 entity-144 (Trimmed Parametric Surface) writer + reader: `write_iges_trimmed_surface(srf, outer_loop, inner_loops) -> bytes` serialises entity 128 (┬з4.26 NURBS surface) wrapped by entity 142 (┬з4.23 Curve on Parametric Surface) outer + optional inner (hole) loops, each referencing entity-126 (┬з4.22) UV-space B-spline curves. `read_iges_trimmed_surface` returns `TrimmedSurfaceRecord` with `outer_loop`, `inner_loops`, `has_3d_outer/inner` flags and `form` (Form 0). Field-count oracle verified against ┬з4.27 Table 1 (4 + N2 fields). Hausdorff round-trip oracle тЙд 1e-6 for trimmed plane + circular-hole case. LLM tool `nurbs_export_iges_144` registered (`geom/io/iges_144_tool.py`); 32 tests green.
- **GK-P reparametrisation** тАФ Reparametrization (chord-length + centripetal + Foley-Nielsen) тЬЕ тАФ `geom/reparam.py`; `fit_curve`/`fit_surface` accept `parameterisation` kwarg; LLM tool `nurbs_reparametrize` registered (Piegl-Tiller ┬з9.2.2).
- **GK-P non-manifold detection + repair** тЬЕ тАФ `detect_non_manifold` / `repair_non_manifold` for B-rep bodies (T-junction edges, touching-cone vertices, self-intersecting loops) and mesh equivalents; `brep_non_manifold_check` + `brep_non_manifold_repair` LLM tools; `heal_body(repair_non_manifold=True)` integration. (Weiler 1985 / Sheffer-Hart 2002.)
- **GK-P curve lifting** тАФ Curve lifting (2D-loop тЖТ 3D-on-surface + inverse) тЬЕ тАФ `geom/curve_lifting.py`: `lift_curve_to_surface`, `lift_curve_with_arc_length`, `project_3d_curve_to_surface_uv`; LLM tool `nurbs_curve_lift_to_surface`; 14 analytic-oracle tests (P&T ┬з10.3.1).
- **GK-P shell-offset operator** тЬЕ тАФ shell-offset operator (constant thickness + fillet propagation): `shell_offset_body`, `detect_shell_self_intersection`, `shell_with_open_face`; `brep_shell_body` LLM tool; 47 tests green.
- **GK-P curvature heatmap export** тЬЕ тАФ `render_curvature_heatmap` / `export_heatmap_png` / `export_heatmap_svg` / `generate_curvature_legend`; viridis + diverging_blue_red palettes; pure-Python PNG encoder (IHDR+IDAT+IEND, no Pillow); 2 LLM tools (`nurbs_export_curvature_png`, `nurbs_export_curvature_svg`) registered тАФ `geom/curvature_heatmap.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CURVATURE-PROFILE-EXPORT** тЬЕ тАФ ╬║(t) sampled along a NurbsCurve at configurable resolution; exports (1) CSV (t, ╬║, arc_length, x, y, z, high_kappa_risk), (2) SVG plot of ╬║ vs arc-length (inflection markers, high-risk bands), (3) PNG plot (pure-Python encoder, no Pillow); `CurvatureProfileResult` dataclass; `export_curvature_profile` / `export_curvature_profile_result`; LLM tool `nurbs_export_curvature_profile` registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; honest-flag `high_kappa_risk` per sample where |d╬║/dt| > 5├Ч mean; 35 hermetic tests (circle oracle ╬║=1/R ┬▒1e-5, S-curve inflection, sin oracle ╬║=|тИТsin t|/(1+cos┬▓t)^(3/2), CSV/SVG/PNG format, degenerate) тАФ Farin ┬з11.6, Sapidis ┬з3 тАФ `geom/curvature_profile_export.py`.
- **GK-P17 SHEET-METAL-FLAT-PATTERN** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_flat_pattern(part: SheetMetalPart) тЖТ FlatPatternResult`; parametric sheet-metal flanges, bends, and unfold-to-flat-pattern with K-factor interpolation from r/t per DIN 6935 / Suchy "Handbook of Die Design" ┬з3 / ANSI Y14.5M. `SheetMetalPart` dataclass: `material` (steel-cold-rolled|stainless-304|aluminum-5052|copper + aliases), `thickness_mm`, `length_mm`, `width_mm`, `bend_radius_mm`, `bend_angle_deg`, `flange_lengths_mm` (ordered straight segments; bends = lenтИТ1). `FlatPatternResult`: `flat_length_mm`, `flat_width_mm`, `bend_allowances_mm` (per-bend BA list), `k_factor`, `total_bend_deduction_mm`, `num_bends`, `honest_caveat`. K-factor interpolation: r/t < 1 тЖТ K = k_min (0.33 steel / 0.31 SS / 0.40 Al/Cu); r/t тЙе 3 тЖТ K = k_max (0.44 steel / 0.38 SS / 0.50 Al/Cu); 1 тЙд r/t < 3 тЖТ linear. BA = (╧А┬╖╬╕/180)┬╖(r + K┬╖t); OSSB = (r+t)┬╖tan(╬╕/2); BD = 2┬╖OSSB тИТ BA; flat_length = ╬гflange_lengths тИТ ╬гBD. LLM tool `sheetmetal_compute_flat_pattern` registered via gated import; re-exported from `kerf_cad_core/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. 33 hermetic tests (K-factor at r/t<1/1/2/3/>3; material alias resolution; single 90┬░ L-bracket KтЙИ0.385; BA formula oracle; flat-length formula oracle; flat-width passthrough; 180┬░ hem fold no-raise; stainless thicker bend K; stainless K < mild steel; U-channel 2 bends; U-channel flat-length formula; zero bends single panel; aluminum K_max; copper alias; unknown material / zero thickness / negative radius / angle>180 / empty flanges тЖТ ValueError; dataclass field types; honest caveat content; re-export from __init__). HONEST CAVEATS: K-factor is empirical (tabulated DIN 6935 interpolation) тАФ measured press-brake data should be used when available; bend-deduction formula assumes inside-set air-bend geometry; bottoming/coining process shifts the neutral axis (see sheet_metal_bend_table.py); spring-back NOT modelled тАФ apply overbend to compensate (typically 1тАУ3┬░ for mild steel per DIN 6935 ┬з4); multi-bend interaction for closely-spaced bends (< 4├Чt apart) not captured; flat_width_mm passed through unchanged (no notch/relief geometry modelled). Refs: Suchy "Handbook of Die Design" ┬з3; DIN 6935:1990; ANSI Y14.5M-2018 тАФ `kerf-cad-core/sheetmetal_features.py`.
- **GK-P16 NURBS-LOFT-WITH-GUIDE-RAILS** тЬЕ тАФ `loft_with_guide_rails(spec: GuideRailLoftSpec) тЖТ GuideRailLoftReport`; skinning loft through cross-section curves while following N guide rail curves that constrain the surface's intermediate shape (Rhino/Fusion 360 guide-rail loft pattern). `GuideRailLoftSpec`: `cross_section_curves` (тЙе 2 NurbsCurves), `guide_rail_curves` (тЙе 1), `num_v_samples` (default 20), `degree_v` (default 3), `closed_v`. `GuideRailLoftReport`: `loft_surface` (NurbsSurface), `num_cross_sections`, `num_guide_rails`, `max_guide_rail_deviation_mm`, `mean_guide_rail_deviation_mm`, `num_self_intersections`, `honest_caveat`. Algorithm: (1) sample v uniformly at `num_v_samples` stations; (2) interpolate cross-sections by lerp between bounding pair; (3) for each guide rail evaluate rail point at v, compute displacement from interpolated cross-section to guide; (4) blend displacement with Gaussian weight centred at the rail's U-parameter (╧Г = 1/(2┬╖n_rails)); (5) accumulate blended displacements; (6) fit interpolating NurbsSurface via row-then-column B-spline fitting (P&T ┬з9.4.5). `_check_guide_endpoint_alignment` warns (UserWarning) when guide endpoints are > 0.5 mm from the first/last cross-section. LLM tool `nurbs_loft_with_guide_rails` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. 28 hermetic tests (cylinder radius consistent, curved guide bulges surface, 3 CS + 2 rails figure-of-8, mismatched endpoint warning, ValueError < 2 CS / < 1 rail, NotImplementedError closed_v, report fields typed, finite CP, max_dev тЙе mean_dev, non-negative self-intersection count, honest caveat non-empty, 4 CS + 3 rails, degree_v clamp, spec defaults, knot clamping, deviation non-negative). HONEST: **approximate** guide-rail constraint тАФ Gaussian displacement blend, NOT an exact constrained-NURBS solver; `max_guide_rail_deviation_mm` and `mean_guide_rail_deviation_mm` are reported for QC; guide endpoints mismatched from cross-sections trigger UserWarning; exact isogeometric constrained fitting (P&T ┬з10.5) is out of scope. Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬з10.3 (skinning) + ┬з10.4 (Gordon); Rhino 8 guide-curve loft docs; Fusion 360 guide-rail loft help тАФ `kerf-cad-core/geom/loft_guide_rails.py`.
- **GK-P15 NURBS-SURFACE-ANALYTIC-DERIVATIVES** тЬЕ тАФ `compute_analytic_derivatives(surface, u, v) тЖТ SurfaceDerivativeResult`; closed-form тИВS/тИВu, тИВS/тИВv, тИВ┬▓S/тИВu┬▓, тИВ┬▓S/тИВuтИВv, тИВ┬▓S/тИВv┬▓ via Piegl & Tiller Algorithm A3.6 (B-spline tensor-product derivative table) + rational quotient rule A4.4. `SurfaceDerivativeResult` dataclass: `dS_du`, `dS_dv`, `d2S_du2`, `d2S_dudv`, `d2S_dv2` (each a `tuple[float,float,float]`), `gauss_K` = (LNтИТM┬▓)/(EGтИТF┬▓), `mean_H` = (ENтИТ2FM+GL)/(2(EGтИТF┬▓)) (do Carmo ┬з3.2; Mortenson ┬з6.5), `honest_caveat`. `SSIHardenedMarcher` class: `march(surface_a, surface_b, seed_uv_a, seed_uv_b, step_mm=0.5, max_steps=1000)` тАФ differential-geometry SSI marcher (Patrikalakis & Maekawa ┬з5) with bisection fallback when |n╠В_A├Чn╠В_B| < tangent_threshold (near-tangent robustness). LLM tool `nurbs_surface_derivatives_analytic` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py`. 19 hermetic tests (plane K=H=0, cylinder K=0/H=1/(2R), sphere K=1/R┬▓/H=1/R, тИВ┬▓S/тИВu┬▓ radially inward on cylinder, analytic vs Richardson FD < 1e-8 non-rational, analytic vs FD < 1e-6 rational cylinder, SSI two-cylinder Steinmetz curve, dataclass fields, rational/non-rational caveats, K=H┬▓ sphere identity, bilinear patch exact partials, parameter clamping, SSI cylinder├Чplane circle radius, near-tangent parallel-plane guard). HONEST: curvature NaN at degenerate points (poles, seams where |S_u├ЧS_v| < 1e-12); rational NURBS uses the correct quotient rule (P&T A4.4) but may have large condition number for near-zero weights; SSI marcher traces one branch per seed тАФ bifurcation points not handled; bisection fallback is O(step┬▓) accurate but uses more evaluations. Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬з3.3 (A3.6/A4.4); Patrikalakis & Maekawa ┬з5; do Carmo ┬з3.2 тАФ `kerf-cad-core/geom/surface_analytic_derivatives.py`.
- **GK-P NURBS-DERIVATIVE-FIELD-VISUAL** тЬЕ тАФ 1st partial-derivative vector-field arrow-plot on NURBS surfaces: `render_derivative_field_png` / `render_derivative_field_svg`; real analytic derivatives at a u/v sample grid (default 12├Ч12) via `surface_derivative`; two-colour encoding (red = тИВS/тИВu, blue = тИВS/тИВv); proper arrow scaling (longest arrow тЙд cell size); pure-Python PNG encoder (IHDR+IDAT+IEND, no Pillow); 2 LLM tools (`nurbs_derivative_field_png`, `nurbs_derivative_field_svg`) registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 19 hermetic tests (flat-plane parallel, sphere tangent, PNG magic bytes, SVG structure, scale bound) тАФ `geom/derivative_field_viz.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-FIT-G2** тЬЕ тАФ `fit_curve_g2(spec: G2FitSpec, degree=5) тЖТ G2FitResult`; fit a degree-5 B-spline curve to a set of 3-D data points with G2 (curvature-continuous) end conditions. `G2FitSpec` dataclass: `data_points` (list of xyz), `start_tangent_xyz`, `start_curvature_xyz`, `end_tangent_xyz`, `end_curvature_xyz`. `G2FitResult`: `fitted_curve` (NurbsCurve), `max_residual_mm`, `mean_residual_mm`, `start_g2_residual`, `end_g2_residual`, `honest_caveat`. Algorithm (Piegl & Tiller ┬з9.4; Farin "CAGD" Ch 10): (1) chord-length parameterisation; (2) clamped knot vector via P&T ┬з9.2 averaging rule; (3) first three and last three control points fixed analytically from the G1/G2 endpoint formulas (P&T Eqs 9.26тАУ9.29: C'(0)=p┬╖(P_1тИТP_0)/╬╛_{p+1}, C''(0)=p(p-1)┬╖[(P_2тИТP_1)/╬╛_{p+2}тИТ(P_1тИТP_0)/╬╛_{p+1}]/╬╛_{p+1}; symmetrically at t=1); (4) interior CPs solved by least-squares collocation. Degree тЙе 2 required for G2; default degree=5. LLM tool `nurbs_fit_curve_g2` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 22 hermetic analytic-oracle tests (straight line residual < 1e-9, circle arc residual < 1e-6, G2 start/end constraints < 1e-9, G1 start/end constraints < 1e-9, 8-point freeform, 12-point 3D, degree-2/3/5, knot clamping, endpoint interpolation, residual non-negativity, residual field parity). HONEST: chord-length parameterisation used throughout тАФ centripetal parameterisation (Lee 1989; Foley-Nielsen 1989) may give smaller oscillations for high-aspect-ratio data with large spacing variation and is NOT implemented here. Curvature vectors are *parametric* second derivatives C''(t), NOT the Frenet curvature ╬║(s)┬╖n╠В тАФ for surface-blending use cases, pass the adjacent curve's C''(t) evaluated at the join parameter тАФ `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_fit_g2.py`. Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬з9.4; Farin "CAGD" Ch 10; Lee (1989) CAD 21(6).
- **NURBS-SURFACE-SHEAR-OFFSET** тЬЕ тАФ `apply_shear_offset(surface, shear: ShearMatrix) тЖТ SurfaceShearOffsetResult`; apply a global linear shear-transform (I+S) to all control points of a NurbsSurface: P'_x = x + s_xy┬╖y + s_xz┬╖z, P'_y = y + s_yx┬╖x + s_yz┬╖z, P'_z = z + s_zx┬╖x + s_zy┬╖y (Mortenson ┬з4.8; Piegl & Tiller ┬з6.1 Theorem 6.1). `ShearMatrix` dataclass: six off-diagonal shear coefficients (s_xy, s_xz, s_yx, s_yz, s_zx, s_zy; all default 0.0). `SurfaceShearOffsetResult`: sheared_surface, max_displacement_mm, mean_displacement_mm, honest_caveat. Knots and weights preserved exactly. LLM tool `nurbs_apply_surface_shear_offset` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 20 hermetic tests (identity unchanged, zero displacement, single-axis oracles for all 6 coefficients, combined superposition, knot/weight preservation, rational weight copy, max/mean displacement formulas, maxтЙеmean invariant, ValueError for non-3D CPs, ShearMatrix defaults, input not mutated, honest caveat content). HONEST: global linear shear only тАФ non-uniform warp (thermal distortion, springback, gravity sag) requires per-point deformation field, not a single ShearMatrix; displacement stats are control-point displacements, not evaluated-surface deviations тАФ `kerf-cad-core/geom/surface_shear_offset.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-FOOTPRINT-ON-PLANE** тЬЕ тАФ `project_curve_to_plane(curve, plane_point, plane_normal) тЖТ FootprintResult`; orthographic projection of a 3-D NurbsCurve onto an arbitrary plane, producing a planar 2-D NurbsCurve in plane-local UV coordinates. `FootprintResult` dataclass: `footprint_curve_2d`, `projection_axis`, `max_orig_depth`, `honest_caveat`. Each control point projected via P' = P тИТ ((PтИТO)┬╖n╠В) n╠В; degree, knot vector and weights preserved exactly (Piegl & Tiller ┬з6.1 Theorem 6.1). Degenerate flag when curve is perpendicular to the plane (footprint collapses to a point). `lift_footprint_to_3d` inverse helper. LLM tool `nurbs_curve_project_to_plane` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 17 hermetic analytic-oracle tests (helixтЖТXY circle radius exact, already-planar identity, vertical-line degenerate, skewed-normal unit-axis, knot/weight/degree preservation, non-rational weights=None, max_orig_depth, projection-formula depth, 45┬░-tilt analytic, make_circle_nurbs round-trip, lift round-trip, ValueError zero-normal, multi-turn helix, YZ-plane analytic). HONEST: orthographic (linear) projection only тАФ no perspective; for rational NURBS the footprint is a correct rational NURBS but the Euclidean evaluated curve may differ from a naive point-by-point projection. Refs: Piegl & Tiller ┬з6.1; Mortenson ┬з4.4 тАФ `kerf-cad-core/geom/curve_footprint_on_plane.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CURVATURE-OSCULATING-CIRCLE** тЬЕ тАФ osculating circle at any parameter t: `osculating_circle(curve, t) тЖТ OsculatingCircle` (center, radius, tangent, curvature, normal_plane_normal, is_degenerate) + `osculating_circles_along(curve, samples)`; ╬║ = |CтА▓├ЧCтА│|/|CтА▓|┬│ (do Carmo ┬з1.5); degenerate sentinel (╬║=0 тЖТ radius=None, is_degenerate=True); LLM tool `nurbs_osculating_circle` registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 18 hermetic tests тАФ circle oracle (╬║=1/R ┬▒1e-6, center=origin), line oracle (╬║=0, degenerate), helix ╬║=0.5/radius=2.0, parabola vertex ╬║=2/radius=0.5, sample-grid тАФ `geom/osculating_circle.py`.
- **NURBS-NORMAL-CURVATURE-AT-POINT** тЬЕ тАФ normal curvature ╬║_n = II(t,t)/I(t,t) via Meusnier's theorem (do Carmo ┬з3.2 / Mortenson ┬з10.4); `normal_curvature_at(srf, u, v, direction_uv) тЖТ NormalCurvatureReport` (╬║_n, ╬║_1, ╬║_2, K, H, principal_dirs, is_umbilic, is_degenerate); principal curvatures from characteristic equation of shape operator; Euler's formula ╬║_n(╬╕)=╬║_1cos┬▓(╬╕-╧Ж)+╬║_2sin┬▓(╬╕-╧Ж) verified; umbilic honest-flag (╬║_1=╬║_2 тЖТ principal_dirs=None); LLM tool `nurbs_normal_curvature_at_point` registered; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; 32 hermetic analytic-oracle tests тАФ sphere K=1/|╬║_n|=1 in 12 dirs, cylinder ╬║_along=0/|╬║_across|=1/R/K=0, saddle K<0/mixed-sign principals, Euler formula bounded in all dirs тАФ `geom/normal_curvature.py`.
- **NURBS-FAIR-COMPOSITE-CURVE** тЬЕ тАФ `composite_fair.py`: `fair_composite(curves, max_iter=50, lambda_smoothness=1.0)` тАФ global curvature-variance fairing for poly-NURBS chains; minimises ╬гтАЦD┬▓PтАЦ┬▓ (discrete bending energy, Greiner-Hormann 1996 ┬з3.2) over all segments with per-iteration G1 seam re-imposition (Klass 1980 ┬з3 bisector) and hard-pinned global endpoints (тЙд1e-6); honest `converged=False` flag for anti-parallel seams or stalled descent; returns `CompositeFairResult` (faired_curves, curvature_variance_before/after, iterations, converged, endpoint_error); `nurbs_fair_composite` LLM tool; 10 hermetic tests тАФ 3-segment kink тЙе50% variance reduction, smooth arc not degraded, endpoints within 1e-6.
- **BREP-CURVE-ON-SURFACE-PROJECTION** тЬЕ тАФ `geom/curve_on_surface_robust.py`; `project_curve_to_surface(curve, surface, tol, samples) -> CurveOnSurfaceResult`; Newton-Raphson with full 2├Ч2 closest-point Jacobian (second-partial terms, Piegl-Tiller ┬з6.1 / PM ┬з3.3); warm-start + coarse-grid seed; near-singular fallback to lstsq; boundary-exit failure detection; UV-trace output as degree-3 NurbsCurve; LLM tool `nurbs_project_curve_to_surface`; 7 hermetic analytic-oracle tests. Honest: no silhouette branch-tracking; Newton stops at local minima; documented.
- **BREP-WIRE-CLOSED-CHECK** тЬЕ тАФ `geom/wire_closed_check.py`; given an ordered list of B-rep edges forming a wire, verify it forms a closed loop (last vertex connects back to first) and check planarity; used as a pre-condition for face creation. `EdgeSegment` dataclass: `start_xyz`, `end_xyz`, `edge_id`; `WireCheckReport` dataclass: `closed`, `planar`, `max_endpoint_gap_mm`, `num_edges`, `plane_normal_xyz`, `max_out_of_plane_deviation_mm`, `honest_caveat`; `check_wire_closed(edges, tolerance_mm=1e-6)` тАФ closed if last.end тЙИ first.start within tol AND every consecutive pair connected; planar via SVD best-fit plane over all endpoints (least singular vector = normal, Pratt 1987; Eberly ┬з6.6). LLM tool `brep_check_wire_closed` registered (gated import); re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`; registered in `plugin.py _TOOL_MODULES`. 26 hermetic analytic-oracle tests (closed square closed=True/planar=True/normal=(0,0,1), open 3-of-4 closed=False, 3-D zig-zag planar=False/max_oop>tol, triangle closed+planar, hexagon closed+planar, square-at-Z5 planar, collinear degenerate, tetrahedron-outline non-planar, lifted vertex non-planar, tolerance sensitivity, empty ValueError, re-export). HONEST: edge order-dependent тАФ scrambled/unordered edge lists are NOT automatically sorted (pass pre-ordered edges only); planarity is endpoint-only (curve interiors are NOT sampled). Refs: Mantyla 'Solid Modeling' ┬з3; Hoffmann ┬з4.

LLM tool: `nurbs_max_deviation_to_mesh`. тЬЕ
- **GK-P auto-lightweight** тАФ Auto-lightweight body (Lyche-M├╕rken knot removal + rational simplification) тЬЕ тАФ `geom/auto_lightweight.py`; `brep_auto_lightweight` LLM tool; 4 hermetic oracle tests.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CIRCLE-FIT** тЬЕ тАФ fit a circle to a 2D NurbsCurve by least-squares (Kasa 1976 + Taubin 1991); reports center, radius, RMS and max residual; `nurbs_fit_circle_to_curve` LLM tool wired. Caveats: 2D only тАФ for 3D space curves project onto a plane first; short arcs (< 30┬░) prefer Taubin. Ref: Taubin (1991) IEEE TPAMI 13(11):1115тАУ1138; Kasa (1976) IEEE TIM 25(1):8тАУ14.
- **NURBS-CURVE-LINE-FIT** тЬЕ тАФ fit a straight line to a 2D NurbsCurve via total-least-squares (TLS) / SVD; `LineFitResult(origin_xy, direction_xy, rms_residual_mm, max_residual_mm, is_planar_line, honest_caveat)`; `fit_line_to_curve` + `nurbs_fit_line_to_curve` LLM tool wired; 35 hermetic tests. Algorithm: centroid subtraction + thin SVD; principal right-singular vector = least-squares line direction; perpendicular residuals computed orthogonally. Use cases: linear-segment detection in imported STEP/IGES profiles, snap-to-line in 2D sketcher, near-straight edge classification. HONEST: 2D only тАФ for 3D space curves project onto a plane first; for 3D principal-axis fit use 3D SVD separately; direction is undirected (unit vector, sign-canonicalised); sampling is parameter-uniform, not arc-length-uniform. Refs: Press ┬з15.7 (TLS); Lawson-Hanson ┬з6 (SVD geometric fitting). `geom/curve_line_fit.py`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.
- **NURBS-CURVE-CONIC-DETECT** тЬЕ тАФ `detect_conic_type(curve_or_points, num_samples=100, residual_threshold_mm=0.01)` returns `ConicDetectResult(conic_type, conic_coefficients, eccentricity, rms_residual_mm, honest_caveat)`; classifies a 2-D NurbsCurve or raw point set as one of: `circle` | `ellipse` | `parabola` | `hyperbola` | `line` | `free_form`. Algorithm: (1) sample `num_samples` 2-D points; (2) line gate тАФ if TLS perpendicular-distance RMS < `residual_threshold_mm` тЖТ `"line"`; (3) fit the general conic Ax┬▓+Bxy+Cy┬▓+Dx+Ey+F=0 via SVD null-space (smallest right-singular vector), normalised so Frobenius norm of the quadratic block [[A, B/2],[B/2, C]] = 1; (4) if RMS pseudo-geometric residual > `residual_threshold_mm` тЖТ `"free_form"`; (5) classify by discriminant ╬Ф = B┬▓тИТ4AC: ╬Ф < тИТ╬╡ тЖТ ellipse-family (circle if additionally |B| < ╬╡_c and |AтИТC| < ╬╡_c┬╖max(|A|,|C|)), |╬Ф| тЙд ╬╡ тЖТ parabola, ╬Ф > ╬╡ тЖТ hyperbola. Eccentricity: 0 for circle, sqrt(1тИТb┬▓/a┬▓) for ellipse, 1 for parabola, sqrt(1+b┬▓/a┬▓) for hyperbola (axes extracted from 3├Ч3 homogeneous conic matrix eigendecomposition). LLM tool `nurbs_detect_conic_type` registered (gated import). Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 32 hermetic tests (circle r=1, circle r=5, ellipse a=3/b=1 eтЙИ0.9428, parabola y=x┬▓/2, horizontal line, tilted line, sinusoid free_form, random free_form, rectangular hyperbola xy=1, coefficient round-trip, raw-point array, threshold gate, degenerate < 5 points). **HONEST CAVEATS**: (1) Algebraic least-squares fit is biased by gradient magnitude тАФ for production-quality circle detection use Pratt (1987) or Taubin (1991) in `curve_circle_fit.py`. (2) Parabola detection via discriminant thresholding is fragile near the parabolic boundary for noisy data тАФ the ╬Ф=0 locus is a measure-zero set. (3) The `rms_residual_mm` is a *pseudo-geometric* residual (algebraic value / gradient magnitude), not the true Euclidean distance to the conic. (4) Line detection uses TLS perpendicular RMS exclusively (degenerate conic Bxy+Dx+Ey+F=0 has nonzero quadratic-block norm, so a separate geometric test is needed). Refs: Pratt, V. (1987) "Direct least-squares fitting of algebraic surfaces." SIGGRAPH ┬з3; Fitzgibbon, A., Pilu, M., & Fisher, R.B. (1999) "Direct least-square fitting of ellipses." IEEE TPAMI 21(5):476тАУ480. `geom/curve_conic_detect.py`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.
- **BREP-EDGE-FACE-NORMAL-FLIP** тЬЕ тАФ detect and fix B-rep faces whose outward normals are inconsistently oriented (some inverted) via iterative neighbour-consensus BFS voting. `FaceNormalFlipResult` dataclass: `face_normals_after`, `num_faces_flipped`, `flipped_face_indices`, `consensus_score`, `honest_caveat`. `detect_and_flip_face_normals(faces_with_normals, max_iter=10, threshold=0.15)`: for each BFS edge (AтЖТB), if dot(n_A, n_B) < -threshold (anti-parallel, indicating face B is inverted relative to the expected co-oriented outward direction of a convex surface) тЖТ flip face B. Iterates until convergence. LLM tool `brep_detect_and_flip_face_normals` registered in `plugin.py`. Re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`. 16 hermetic tests. **Honest caveats**: (1) PERPENDICULAR-FACE LIMITATION тАФ adjacent faces with orthogonal normals (|dot|тЙдthreshold, e.g. unit cube) produce no flip signal; a cube cannot be corrected from normals alone. (2) Algorithm assumes CONVEX surface convention (adjacent outward normals co-oriented, dot>0); NOT valid for concave surfaces or open flat meshes where inversion produces co-oriented pairs. (3) Isolated faces (no neighbour_face_indices) are returned unchanged. (4) Absolute orientation is seeded from the first face per connected component тАФ all-inward input is internally consistent but absolutely wrong. (5) Not a geometric B-rep heal: does not recompute normals from surface derivatives; for production use OCCT BRepLib::OrientClosedSolid. Refs: Mantyla ┬з6.4; Hoffmann ┬з3; Weiler 1985 ┬з3. `geom/face_normal_flip.py`; re-exported from `geom/__init__.py`.

- **T-101 CFD depth** тАФ T-101-A k-╬╡ тЬЕ; T-101-B 3-D unstructured meshing тЬЕ; T-101-C OpenFOAM bridge тЬЕ (case generator, polyMesh writer, result parser, LLM tools).
- **T-100 FEM depth** тАФ explicit dynamics (module exists, not yet imported/registered); full nonlinear static (only 1-D bar/truss shipped); k-╬╡ turbulence CFD; coupled FEA-based variation analysis. (Acoustics FEM, EM, harmonic, buckling, PSD, multi-axial fatigue are now shipped.)
- **T-101 CFD depth** тАФ RANS turbulence models тЬЕ; 3-D unstructured meshing тЬЕ; OpenFOAM bridge export adapter тЬЕ (T-101-C complete тАФ `export_to_openfoam` + `cfd_export_openfoam` LLM tool; file export only, user must have OpenFOAM 11).
- **AFR topology ordering** тАФ promote the AAG feature classifier output into a fully replay-able parametric DAG (depends on NURBS kernel completeness).
- **Reverse-engineering freeform fit** тАФ freeform NURBS surface fit from segmented point clouds; currently only analytic primitives (plane/sphere/cylinder/cone/torus).
- **AFR topology ordering** тАФ promote the AAG feature classifier output into a fully replay-able parametric DAG (depends on NURBS kernel completeness).
- **PLM configurator layer** тАФ 150%/effectivity BOM, where-used, ECR/ECO workflow, MBSE/SysML traceability.
- **PLM configurator layer** тАФ configurator + effectivity BOM тЬЕ shipped (`kerf-plm`); remaining: where-used, ECR/ECO workflow, MBSE/SysML traceability.
- **PLM configurator layer** тАФ 150%/effectivity BOM, where-used, ECR/ECO workflow. (MBSE digital thread / SysML 1.x XMI traceability тЬЕ shipped тАФ `kerf-plm`.)
- **KBE general configurator** тАФ rule-driven design configurator layer on top of the existing standard-specific compliance engines.
- **KBE general configurator** тЬЕ тАФ general `KBEEngine` with 10-rule starter pack (AISC W-shape, ACI rebar, ASCE 7 wind, ISO 281 bearing, ASME B106 shaft, NEC wire/breaker/transformer, IPC pipe, Darcy-Weisbach pump) + `kbe_apply_rules` LLM tool. Deep multi-domain configurator integration (BOM routing, variant management) still ahead.
- **PLM configurator layer** тАФ where-used, ECR/ECO workflow, MBSE/SysML traceability (variant configurator + KBE bridge shipped тЬЕ in `kerf-plm`).
- **KBE general configurator** тАФ KBE engine + configurator bridge shipped тЬЕ; remaining: BOM routing variants, 150%-BOM expansion, variant management UI.

### Needs UI / deploy-gated

- **P0-8 deploy-hardening** тАФ realistic seed data + one-command dev loop; test coverage breadth still expanding.
- **P1-7 formboard flatten** тЬЕ тАФ shipped in T-37: `formboard_flatten.py` + `wiring_formboard_flatten` LLM tool; topological unfold with branch alternation, connector pinouts, bbox; waypoints complete тЬЕ тАФ every branch traversal (including simple two-node stubs) now emits BranchPoint2D for tap AND tip.
- **P1-8 large-file git** тАФ pointer kind + Phase 1 shipped; deduplication-based free-fork accounting and content-addressed LFS store in progress.
- ~~**G-5 class-A wiring**~~ тЬЕ frontend wiring shipped тАФ see G-5 row above.
- **Long-tail verticals** тАФ see "Long-tail verticals" list above; all committed, none started.

---

## Deliberately not building

This list is only AI-redundant *authoring/UX interaction paradigms* тАФ not skipped domains or correctness features.

| Not building | Why |
|---|---|
| Visual node programming (Grasshopper / Dynamo / Sverchok) | The LLM writing a parametric script *is* the graph. `.script.py` + SDKs + JSCAD + `.graph` cover the value. |
| Ribbon / toolbar maximalism | The LLM is the command palette тАФ discovery is a chat sentence, not a menu hunt. |
| Macro recorders / scripting-GUI builders | The LLM is the macro author; it writes `.script.py` directly. |
| Gumball / direct-modeling maximalism | Keep a basic gumball; the LLM edits the feature tree. |
| In-app wizards / tutorials / onboarding tours | The chat is the wizard тАФ context-specific guidance on demand. |

---

## How to contribute

Pick a task from [`tasks.md`](./tasks.md) (sized for a single isolated agent run), or open an issue proposing a new long-tail sector line. The roadmap states *why* and *in what order*; `tasks.md` is the *how*. Keep them in sync: when a priority moves here, move the corresponding tasks there.
